# GPU тАФ hexa-lang's NVPTX-first GPU substrate (domain SSOT)

> One-file roadmap + cycle ledger for the GPU codegen substrate
> (RFC 055 + RFC 067/068/069 chain + ongoing follow-ons). Domain
> SSOT per `AGENTS.tape` `@D g_plan_consolidation`: cycle-by-cycle
> progression appended to `compiler/PLAN.md`; this file is the
> *forward-looking checklist* + *brainstorm-to-exhaustion roadmap*.

**hexa-lang North-Star тСа (NN stack)** + **┬з12 P4+ chain** + **GOAL тАФ "cuBLAS-using stacks ые╝ whole-program-fusion ьЬ╝ыбЬ ьЪ░эЪМ"** are the umbrella metrics this file tracks.

---

## 0 ┬╖ One-paragraph state (end-of-day 2026-05-20)

┬з12 P4+ chain end-to-end functional: codegen-side (hexa MIR тЖТ PTX) and silicon-side (PTX тЖТ ptxas тЖТ RTX 5070 sm_120 driver-JIT тЖТ numeric correctness) both **measured-PASS**. 25 PRs landed today including the **first three ever ┬з12 P4+ silicon-fire closures** (RFC 067 WMMA, RFC 068 f16, RFC 069 unroll byte-eq) + codegenтЖФsilicon reconcile (PR #193). `nvptx_lower_test` smoke: 9/9 тЖТ 25/25 cases this session.

---

## 1 ┬╖ Completed (measured-PASS, landed on origin/main)

### 1a тАФ codegen scaffolding (RFC 055 ┬з1-┬з12 P3)

- [x] **RFC 055 Stage-1 scaffold** тАФ NVPTX target enum, PTX opcode table, address-space constants, target enum dispatch
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P0** тАФ PTX text emit pass for FP64-arithmetic subset (`add.f64`, `mul.f64`, `mov.f64`, `ret`, `.func`, `.reg .f64`)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P1** тАФ `@gpu_kernel` end-to-end vec-add slice (`.visible .entry`, `.param .u64`, `ld.global.f64`, `st.global.f64`, `mov.u32 %tid.x`, address arithmetic, bounds-check `setp + bra`)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P2** тАФ naive FP64 GEMM `@gpu_kernel` (i-j-k loop, FMA-ready)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P3a** тАФ `--target=nvptx64-nvidia-cuda-sm{80,90}` dispatch in `compiler/main.hexa`
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P3b** тАФ per-Local PTX register-kind classification (`.f64` / `.u32` / `.u64` / `.pred`)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P3b** тАФ `STMT_BR` / `STMT_BR_COND` / `STMT_CALL gpu_*` / `STMT_LOAD` / `STMT_STORE` generic lowering
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P3c** тАФ `@gpu_kernel` / `@gpu_device` partition (`gpu_kind` field on `MFunc`)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P4** тАФ `gpu_barrier()` block-wide sync (`bar.sync 0;`)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P4+** тАФ `gpu_atomic_add()` global `atom.add.f64`
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P4+** тАФ `gpu_warp_shuffle()` `shfl.sync.idx.b32`
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P4+** тАФ Tensor Core MMA scaffold (NVPTX_RKIND_FRAG, `_nvptx_wmma_mnemonic` table, STMT_CALL recognition)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P4+** тАФ mixed-precision scaffold (NVPTX_RKIND_F16/_BF16/_F32, classifier rules)
- [x] **RFC 055 055-P4+** тАФ `_nvptx_unroll_pass` MVP (canonical 3-block back-edge, factor=2)

### 1d тАФ RFC 069 (advanced loop unroll)

- [x] **P0** тАФ Shape-B RFC draft + marker comments (PR #141)

- [x] **P4 silicon** тАФ unroll=1 vs unroll=2 vec-add byte-eq on RTX 5070, `byte_mismatch=0/1024`, `F-RFC069-NUMERIC-EQ` PASS (PR #190)

### 1f тАФ Crash-recovery cycle (2026-05-21)

Recovery cycle after macOS crash lost two in-flight stash diffs (rounds 5-8 GPU.md doc + RFC 071 P2.1 spec, both unpushed). The original artifact directories referenced from those stashes (`rfc067_p9_rounds_5_7_2026_05_21/`, `rfc067_pA_round8_2026_05_21/`, `rfc067_p6_revalidate_2026_05_21/`) were lost system-wide. Stash patches preserved at `docs/notes/crash_recovery_2026_05_21/`. Re-fired the idempotent subset on ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120; new artifact: `archive/fires/rfc067_pB_crash_recovered_2026_05_21/`.

- [x] **F-RFC067-PB-ORACLE-BATTERY** тАФ 8/9 hand-emit PTX smokes ptxas_rc=0 on ubu-2 (sm_80 + sm_90 mixed): `vprintf` ┬╖ `__assertfail` ┬╖ `atom.shared.add.s32` ┬╖ `ldmatrix.sync.aligned.x4.m8n8.shared.b16` ┬╖ `mbarrier.init.shared::cta.b64` (sm_90) ┬╖ `wmma.mma.sync...m16n16k16.f16.f16` ┬╖ `wmma.mma.sync...m16n16k16.f32.bf16.bf16.f32` ┬╖ `bar.sync 0` (coop_launch). 1 honest fail: `cp.async.bulk.shared::cta.global` тЖТ "State space incorrect" (TMA needs full tensor descriptor + mbarrier rendezvous, not the bulk-copy primitive in isolation). - [x] **F-RFC075-METAL-SHAPES-SCALEUP-NUMERIC-EQ** ЁЯЫ╕ тАФ 3-shape ├Ч 7-size scale-up on Apple M3: vec_add / vec_mul / vec_scale ├Ч NтИИ{1K, 4K, 16K, 64K, 256K, 1M, 4M}. 5 warmup + 50 timed dispatches per (shape, N). **21/21 byte_eq with CPU reference**. Peak effective bandwidth at N=4M: vec_mul **39.94 GB/s** ┬╖ vec_add **34.59 GB/s** ┬╖ vec_scale **22.34 GB/s** (lower because `vec_scale.metal` is hardcoded with 3-buffer dispatch ABI but only reads buf-a + writes buf-c тАФ formula `3┬╖N┬╖4/median` overcounts; corrected 2┬╖N┬╖4 would put vec_scale around 14.89 GB/s, consistent with bytes-moved). Re-measured vec_add 4M = 34.59 GB/s vs earlier (commit `9ee6d020`) 50.53 GB/s тАФ system state drift (thermal / scheduling), both honest. Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc075_metal_shapes_scaleup_2026_05_21/`
- [x] **F-RFC067-COOKBOOK-SASS-DIFF (full 6-shape)** тАФ Per-shape hexa-emit vs nvcc CUDA C reference SASS instruction count comparison across all 6 cookbook WMMA kernels (extends commit `a1f9d80b`'s step1-only diff). nvcc 12.0.140 + cuobjdump on ubu-2 RTX 5070. Results: **step1_single_tile 80=80 (1.000 equal)** ┬╖ **step2_multitile 320 vs 272 (1.176 hexa heavier +17.6%)** ┬╖ **step3_multiwarp 336 vs 416 (0.808 hexa leaner тИТ19.2%)** ┬╖ **step4_cp_async 256 vs 928 (0.276 non-comparable тАФ nvcc uses `cuda::pipeline` + `cooperative_groups::memcpy_async` state machine; hexa uses raw `cp.async.cg` + `wait_all`)** ┬╖ **step5_tf32 144=144 (1.000 equal тАФ was nvcc-generated)** ┬╖ **composite_perf 352 vs 416 (0.846 hexa leaner тИТ15.4%)**. Across 5 directly-comparable shapes: **hexa SASS 0.81-1.18├Ч nvcc** (typical codegen variation). Stash 1's "hexa 53.9% of nvcc SASS" claim conclusively **REFUTED** across the full cookbook. Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc067_pE_cookbook_sass_diff_2026_05_21/` (6├Ч `step<N>_ref.cu` + `.cubin` + `.ptx` + `result.json`)
- [x] **F-RFC075-METAL-SUBDIV-NUMERIC-EQ** ЁЯЫ╕ тАФ vec-sub + vec-div MIR shapes silicon-validated on Apple M3 (cherry-pick `ca49aea1` from N2 sub-agent worktree, codegen now recognises **5 shapes**: vec-add + vec-mul + vec-sub + vec-div + vec-scale). `vec_sub` (3-buffer) **byte-eq** (max|╬Ф|=0, byte_mismatch=0/1024). `vec_div` **тЙд1 ULP** (max_ulp=1, 284/1024 cells deviate by тЙд1 ULP) тАФ Apple M3 GPU likely decomposes IEEE FP32 divide into `rcp + mul`, which is the standard GPU compromise (cuBLAS / Metal Performance Shaders both do this; not a codegen issue). Falsifier PASS criterion = byte-eq for arith with no decomposition + тЙд4 ULP for divide. Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc075_metal_subdiv_2026_05_21/` (vec_sub.metal/.air/.metallib + vec_div.metal/.air/.metallib + host_subdiv.swift + result.json)
- [x] **F-RFC067-HGEMM-SCALEUP-HEXA (full 5-shape via shape-port)** тАФ N4 sub-agent fired hand-emit PTX variants `wmma_{384,512,768,1024}x{...}_grid.ptx` produced by scaling the 256-shape's address-arithmetic constants + WMMA stride operands (microcode + 16-warp 4├Ч4 block layout identical across all 5). Re-measured 5-shape ratios on ubu-2 RTX 5070 (200 timed launches per shape, 20 warmup, `cudaEventRecord` per-iter sync): **M=256 ratio 0.767** ┬╖ **M=384 ratio 0.740** ┬╖ **M=512 ratio 0.417** ┬╖ **M=768 ratio 0.350** ┬╖ **M=1024 ratio 0.287**. Hexa TFLOPS: 3.50 ┬╖ 9.67 ┬╖ 10.42 ┬╖ 16.69 ┬╖ 15.61. cuBLAS TFLOPS: 4.56 ┬╖ 13.06 ┬╖ 24.97 ┬╖ 47.66 ┬╖ 54.34. **Monotonic degradation** as M grows тАФ naive K-loop is bandwidth-bound, lacks shared-memory tiling + software pipelining + async copies + split-K. Matches the optimiser-gap pattern documented in `reference_ptx_diff_perf_oracle` memory. M=256 ratio 0.767 matches commit `d9b737a2` (methodology stability across two fires). Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc067_pD_hgemm_followon_2026_05_21/` (host.c 440 lines + 4 new PTX + result.json). Honest scope: 4 new PTX are HAND-emit (not from compiler codegen); compiler `nvptx_target.hexa` still shape-locked at 256 тАФ variable-M emission via the same compiler path is a follow-on (would benefit from RFC 071 P3 module-loader bridge to drive MIR тЖТ PTX from source); no numeric correctness check at new shapes (timing only тАФ shape-port preserves WMMA microcode so correctness inherits from M=256)
- [x] **F-RFC071-SM-ARCH-THREADED** тАФ RFC 071 P2.2 cherry-pick from N6 sub-agent worktree (commit `f7a7404f`). - [x] **F-RFC075-METAL-REDUCE-SUM-NUMERIC-EQ + CODEGEN INTEGRATION** ЁЯЫ╕ тАФ Apple M3 silicon-fire + codegen integration both landed. Silicon side: N=1024 input filled with `1.0`s, threadgroup=32 тЖТ 32 per-SIMD-group outputs, all **exactly 32.0** (byte-eq, max|╬Ф|=0.0, byte_mismatch=0/32). Hand-emit `reduce_sum.metal` uses Apple's `simd_sum` + lane-0 gated per-group write. Codegen side: N5-retry sub-agent commit `78b0e489` cherry-picked as `402ef897` тАФ `compiler/codegen/metal_target.hexa` now recognises **6 shapes** (vec-add + vec-mul + vec-sub + vec-div + vec-scale + **reduce-sum** тАФ the FIRST non-element-wise shape). New `_metal_mfunc_is_reduce_sum_shape` recogniser + `_metal_emit_reduce_kernel_signature` (2-buffer, NOT 3-buffer) + `_metal_emit_reduce_sum_body` (simd_sum + lane-0 gated `c[group_id] = v`). New `metal_lower_test.hexa` Case 9 PASS. Build + run all 9 cases PASS (sub-agent verified `hexa build` + `/tmp/metal_lower_test_n5` runs to completion). Mechanism: **register footprint 32тЖТ70 regs/thread** (32 fp32 accumulators + 16 fragment regs + pipeline temps); reg/CTA 70├Ч512=35840 тЖТ only **1 CTA/SM fits** (RTX 5070 = 65536 regs/SM); vs N66 PK 32├Ч512=16384 тЖТ 4 CTAs/SM. **Occupancy collapse 4├Ч** wipes the 4├Ч per-warp compute amortisation. ptxas info: 70 regs/thread, 16384 B smem, **0 spill** uniform across shapes. Follow-up candidates: 4-warp 32├Ч32 CTA (64├Ч64 output, fewer warps, vectorised cp.async size=16) + `.maxnreg 32` to force spill over occupancy collapse + `ldmatrix`-based sharedтЖТfragment. Collapsed to single `.reg .b32 %rb<6>;` and renamed `%rb20тЖТ%rb4`, `%rb21тЖТ%rb5`. Swizzle pattern: `phys_col = log_col XOR (log_row & 7)` applied symmetrically on cp.async store + consumer load. XOR self-inverse so round-trip preserves semantics. **Useful partial negative (`@D g3`)**: 2 changes bundled (XOR swizzle + mma path swap to `mma.sync.m16n8k8 ├Ч 2`). The +6% over N66 PK can NOT be attributed solely to XOR тАФ likely the 2-mma manual-fragment path adds overhead partly cancelling swizzle gain, consistent with -7% vs N74. **Conclusion**: bank-conflict swizzling on RTX 5070 sm_120 is **measurable but not dominant**; vector cp.async (N74) remains stronger single-axis win on this substrate. - [x] **F-RFC071-NVPTX-SHFL-BFLY-B32 (N71-A, `9d21356c` + `7671d7db`)** ЁЯЫ╕ тАФ `gpu_warp_shuffle_xor(v, lane_mask) -> u32` wired to NVPTX codegen. Emits `shfl.sync.bfly.b32 %r<dst>, %r<src>, %r<mask>, 0x1f, 0xffffffff;`. `bfly` mode XORs caller's lane id with mask operand тЖТ canonical primitive for warp-reduce butterfly (mask = 16, 8, 4, 2, 1 reduces 32 lanes pairwise). `0x1f` lane-mask+clamp-mode selector (full warp); `0xffffffff` membermask covering all 32 warp lanes (CUDA __FULL_MASK). Mirrors `gpu_warp_shuffle` shape тАФ same U32 dst bank, same `%r<id>` register operands. **NEW const**: `PTX_OP_SHFL_SYNC_BFLY_B32`. **Classifier rule** added тЖТ NVPTX_RKIND_U32. Register count: 38/thread (vs N76 30 = +8 for NXT frags; well under 64 budget тАФ NO occupancy collapse). **Mechanism FALSIFIED**: ptxas (CUDA 12.0) reordered SASS тАФ PTX intent `ldmatrix NXT тЖТ ldmatrix NXT тЖТ mma CUR тЖТ mma CUR` but observed SASS at K-loop body shows `HMMA тЖТ LEA тЖТ HMMA тЖТ LDSM (after HMMA) тЖТ LDSM`. ptxas saw `rA,rB` written AFTER mma reads `ra,rb`, so all 4 instructions def-use-independent тЖТ chose alternate ordering minimizing live-range overlap. **Static PTX-level overlap invisible to scheduling control**. **3 explanations consistent with null**: (1) ptxas auto-pipelines cross-iteration regardless of static schedule (2) mma is NOT bottleneck at MтЙе768 (currently 23% of RTX 5070 134 TFLOPS HGEMM peak; cuBLAS at 50% = 2.16├Ч gap too large for ldmatrix latency hiding alone) (3) RTX 5070 sm_120 may OoO-issue independent LDSM/HMMA pipes regardless of static ordering. **Remaining N76-list candidates**: single-buffered D output staging + K-loop unroll for ILP + larger output tile (64├Ч64 тЖТ 128├Ч128). - [ ] **F-RFC067-HEXA-SGEMM-MMA-M16N8K32 (N90, ISA-LAYER FALSIFIED)** тАФ **HARDWARE-ILLEGAL shape for FP16 multiplicands on all NVIDIA tensor-core generations through Blackwell sm_120**. ptxas rejects `mma.sync.aligned.m16n8k32.f32.f16.f16.f32` with `Illegal matrix shape '.m16n8k32' for instruction 'mma'` on **all 6 shapes / all arch targets (sm_90/90a/120/120a) / all ptxas versions (12.0.140, 12.9.86, driver-JIT 13000)**. Sanity cross-check with `m16n8k32.s32.s8.s8.s32` got DIFFERENT error (vector-size mismatch) тЖТ confirms ptxas accepts `.m16n8k32` shape token, but only for sub-byte int types. **Root cause (PTX ISA 8.7 ┬з9.7.13.4.13)**: `m16n8k32` defined exclusively for sub-byte integer multiplicands (`.s8`/`.u8`/`.s4`/`.u4`/`.b1`). K-doubling comes from packing more sub-byte elements into same register footprint тАФ **physically impossible for 2-byte FP16**. FP16 supported shapes only: `m8n8k4`, `m16n8k8`, `m16n8k16`. **Falsification more fundamental than target-bump** (task's honest-scope category): instruction simply doesn't exist for FP16 on any NVIDIA HW. **Peak TFLOPS N/A** (6/6 PTX load failures at driver-JIT, kernel never launched). cuBLAS re-measured 67.13 TFLOPS @ M=1536 (matches N77 baseline within variance). N77 36.06 / ratio 0.533 remains current `mma.sync`-path peak. **Path forward for "more arithmetic per mma issue on FP16"**: Hopper `wgmma.mma_async.sync.aligned` (sm_90+) or Blackwell `tcgen05.mma` (sm_100+) тАФ different instruction classes (descriptor-based shared mem + async pipelining + different reg allocation). NOT a drop-in shape swap; multi-session refactor. Within `mma.sync` semantics, remaining levers: CTA output-tile (currently 64├Ч64), pipeline depth (currently 2-slot DB), ldmatrix layout. Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc067_pT_hexa_sgemm_m16n8k32_2026_05_21/` (PTX pure-ASCII addressing math correct; only mma instruction itself ISA-illegal)

- [x] **ЁЯЫ╕ F-RFC067-NVPTX-TMA-CODEGEN-SCAFFOLD PASS (N202, codegen scaffold тАФ opcodes + sm_120a header emit + req doc, zero behavior change)** тАФ TMA codegen wiring scaffold in the compiler. 3 files (+583 -3): (1) NEW `compiler/codegen/nvptx_tma_ops.hexa` (~220 lines) тАФ sibling of `nvptx_ptx_ops.hexa`, enumerates 6 TMA opcode constants (`CP_ASYNC_BULK_TENSOR_2D/5D`, `MBARRIER_INIT/ARRIVE_EXPECT_TX/TRY_WAIT_PARITY`, `FENCE_PROXY_ASYNC_SHARED_CTA`, `CVTA_PARAM_U64`), sm_120a+8.7 arch gate, CUtensorMap ABI constants (128B/align-64/max-rank-5), feature-flag predicate `nvptx_tma_codegen_enabled()` defaulting `false`, stub header emitter `nvptx_emit_module_header_for_tma(target_sm)` (2) `nvptx_lower_test.hexa` case 32 (3) NEW `docs/notes/2026-05-22-tma-runtime-builtin-requirements.md` (~190 lines) тАФ host-side `cuTensorMapEncodeTiled` runtime-builtin requirements + integration point with N128 WMMA matmul lane. **32/32 lower_test PASS** (was 31/31). **CPU codegen MD5-identical** (arm64_darwin, x86_64_linux, nvptx_target.hexa byte-identical). Feature flag default `false` = byte-identical existing emit path. Integration site: `_nvptx_emit_matmul_module` (N203+ adds third dispatch axis). Artifact: commit on origin/main.
- [x] **ЁЯЫ╕ЁЯЫ╕ЁЯЫ╕ЁЯЫ╕ F-RFC067-NVPTX-TMA-SOURCE-TO-SILICON PASS (N206, TMA source-to-silicon E2E CLOSED on consumer Blackwell)** тАФ Flipped N202's feature flag + wired full TMA codegen dispatch. Feature flag `nvptx_tma_codegen_enabled()` reads `HEXA_NVPTX_TMA=1` env via hexa builtin `env_var` (NOT `getenv` тАФ collides with libc). Dispatch wiring in `compiler/codegen/nvptx_target.hexa` (+182 -6): extended `_nvptx_arch_for_target` / `_nvptx_target_tag_for_sm_arch` / `_nvptx_ptx_version_for_sm_arch` with sm_120a branch (PTX 8.7); 4-line gate in `_nvptx_emit_matmul_module` (line 4830); new `pub fn _nvptx_emit_matmul_tma_module` (~155 lines) emitting SMOKE-level TMA kernel (header + shared mem + 2 TMA descriptors + cvta.param.u64 chain + mbarrier ops + cp.async.bulk.tensor.2d + fence.proxy.async + K-loop + write-back). **33/33 lower_test PASS** both flag states (case 32 + new case 33). **CPU codegen UNCHANGED** (only NVPTX files touched). **ubu-1 RTX 5070 silicon-fire PASS**: codegen-emitted `sgemm_tma_codegen.ptx` (104 lines) тЖТ mismatch=0/256, verdict=TMA_SMOKE_PASS. **TMA source-to-silicon E2E CLOSED on consumer Blackwell** (codegen-emit half). Honest scope: SMOKE-level only (full mma.sync chain + Hilbert from N200-full not yet codegen-emitted); `gpu_tma_encode_tiled_2d` host-side runtime builtin not yet implemented (host uses CUDA Driver API directly per N202 req doc). Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc067_n206_tma_codegen_emit_2026_05_22/`

- N=1024 (small); larger N + multi-threadgroup + reductions are follow-on cycles
- No perf measurement тАФ silicon-fire correctness only; Metal vs cuBLAS / Metal Performance Shaders perf comparison is a separate cycle

### 1h тАФ F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH: fused attention moat (structural-formal + wall ruled-out) (2026-05-25)

The ┬з10 moat case cuBLAS structurally CANNOT do: a single fused flash-attention kernel computing `softmax(Q K^T/тИЪd) V` with online-softmax tiling (running max + running sum), **never materializing the N├ЧN score matrix S to HBM**. Hand-emit pure-ASCII PTX (`archive/fires/fusion_attention_flash_2026_05_25/flash_attn.ptx`), fired on ubu-2 RTX 5070 (sm_120, driver 580) against a cuBLAS-using baseline (`cublasGemmStridedBatchedEx` QK^T тЖТ write S тЖТ standalone softmax kernel тЖТ `cublasGemmStridedBatchedEx` ┬╖V). GPU uncontended at fire time (0% util, no compute procs тЖТ timed wall taken, not deferred). **Verdict: ЁЯФ╡ structural-formal + ЁЯФ┤ wall axis ruled-out (g3 closed-negative тАФ both terminal, both publishable).**

- [x] **F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH structural (clause a)** ЁЯФ╡ тАФ PROVEN closed-form. fused **1 launch** vs baseline **3**; S-matrix HBM round-trip fused **0 B** vs baseline **4┬╖N┬▓┬╖4 B** (O(N┬▓) eliminated). Total-HBM ratio `R(N,d) = (5Nd+4N┬▓)/(4Nd) = 1.25 + N/d` тЖТ **9.25├Ч @512, 17.25├Ч @1024, 33.25├Ч @2048, 65.25├Ч @4096** (d=64). hexa-native compiled `ratio_check.hexa` reproduces R exactly (`4├ЧR(2048,64)=133 тЗТ 33.25`) тЖТ **ЁЯФ╡ SUPPORTED-FORMAL**. $0 structural oracle (`structural_oracle.c`, deterministic, no GPU) is the PRIMARY finding. Verdict: `.verdicts/fusion-attention-flash/F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH.txt`
- [x] **F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH ptxas-clean** тАФ `flash_attn.ptx` pure-ASCII; `ptxas -arch=sm_80` rc=0, `-arch=sm_90` rc=0; driver-JIT load on sm_120 (`cuModuleLoadDataEx`, `CU_JIT_TARGET_FROM_CUCONTEXT`) rc=0
- [x] **F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH-NUMERIC** тАФ fused output vs **f64 CPU reference** rel-err тЙд 1e-2 PASS at NтИИ{512,1024,2048,4096} d=64 (max_rel ~1e-6, three orders under tol). Baseline matches identically (validates the layout)
- [x] **F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH wall (clause b) тАФ ЁЯФ┤ FALSIFIED (ruled-out axis)** тАФ cudaEvent, 20 warmup + 200 timed, median ms. fused(1 launch) vs baseline(3 launch): **0.415 vs 0.282 @512 ┬╖ 0.823 vs 0.559 @1024 ┬╖ 1.640 vs 1.143 @2048 ┬╖ 3.788 vs 2.492 @4096**. The cuBLAS baseline is **1.4тАУ1.5├Ч FASTER at every shape**. The fused kernel is a naive 1-thread-per-query scalar online-softmax; cuBLAS runs QK^T and ┬╖V on Tensor Cores. **Closed-negative: structural fusion ALONE does not win wall vs cuBLAS** тАФ the moat (1 launch, 0 S-HBM) is necessary but NOT sufficient. The тЙе30% wall additionally requires the fused inner GEMMs at Tensor-Core throughput (wmma m16n8k* tiling over Q/K/V blocks, S in shared memory). This deterministically scopes the next cycle.
- [ ] **┬з10 box "Whole-program-fusion тЙе30%" stays `[ ]`** тАФ structural-only; the wall was measured and NOT won (g3 honesty тАФ structural-only / closed-negative leaves the box open with the finding noted). ┬з5b "Attention scoring fusion" remains `[ ]` pending the Tensor-Core fused kernel.

g3 caveats:
- The wall negative is specific to the NAIVE scalar fused kernel тАФ it does NOT falsify the moat thesis; it falsifies "fusion alone suffices" and pre-registers the Tensor-Core fused-attention kernel as the next falsifier
- d=64 single-head, FP32 throughout (the GEMMs are small enough that the O(N┬▓) S round-trip the baseline pays is not large vs its TC GEMM speed); longer-context / multi-head / fp16 may shift the crossover and is a follow-on
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile changes (@F f2) тАФ CPU codegen files MD5-identical pre/post (`self/runtime.c`, `compiler/codegen/{x86_64_linux,arm64_darwin}.hexa` unchanged); the fire is hand-emit PTX + .c hosts only

### 1h тАФ Whole-program-fusion epilogue: GEMM + bias + GeLU structural finding (2026-05-25) ЁЯЫ╕

The classic fused-epilogue case cuBLAS cannot do: GEMM + bias-add + GeLU activation in one kernel. A single hexa-emit kernel computing `C = GeLU(A@B + bias)` fuses the GEMM, the bias-add, and the GeLU into one epilogue and writes the M├ЧN result to HBM ONCE. This is a `$0`-oracle + ptxas-clean codegen round; the **timed silicon fire is DEFERRED to a serial follow-up** (ubu-2 is shared тАФ parallel timed fires contend and poison wall numbers). Branch `gpu-fusion-epilogue` (from origin/main `49fcf884`). Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_epilogue_gemm_bias_gelu_2026_05_25/`.

- [x] **F-FUSION-EPILOGUE-GEMM-BIAS-GELU (structural oracle, PRIMARY finding)** ЁЯФ╡ тАФ `$0` deterministic launch/byte count (`tool/fusion_epilogue_structural_oracle.hexa`, compiled hexa, run on ubu-1). At the LLaMA-7B FFN shape (M=4096 N=11008 K=4096; C tensor 180 355 072 B): **FUSED = 1 launch + 1├Ч M├ЧN HBM C-write** vs **BASELINE (cuBLAS-using stack: `cublasSgemm` тЖТ bias-add kernel тЖТ GeLU kernel) = 3 launches + 3├Ч M├ЧN HBM C-write**. **launch reduction 66.667 % AND HBM-write reduction 66.667 %** тАФ both clear the тЙе30 % whole-program-fusion gate by construction. Shape-independent (256┬│ cross-check identical, since the C-write traffic depends only on M├ЧN). Verdict persisted `.verdicts/fusion-epilogue-gemm-bias-gelu/fusion_epilogue_structural.txt`
- [x] **F-FUSION-EPILOGUE-PTXAS-CLEAN** ЁЯФ╡ тАФ `ptxas -arch=sm_80 fused_gemm_bias_gelu.ptx` on ubu-2 (CUDA 12.0): **RC=0, 23 registers, 0 spill, 4264-byte cubin**. PTX pure ASCII, md5 `1d7380556da101b7e37017b79eed6f01`. GeLU via tanh-approx (`ex2.approx.f32` base-2 exp + `rcp.approx.f32`), GEMM FP32 `fma.rn.f32`, bias-add + activation fused before the single `st.global.f32`
- [ ] **F-FUSION-EPILOGUE-WALL (timed advantage, DEFERRED-to-serial-follow-up)** тАФ fused 1-launch kernel wall vs the 3-launch cuBLAS-using baseline wall on ubu-2 RTX 5070. Host launchers authored (`tool/fusion_epilogue_fused_host.c` 1-launch driver-API + `tool/fusion_epilogue_cublas_baseline.c` 3-launch cuBLAS stack, both rel-err тЙд1e-2 vs f64 CPU ref). DEFERRED тАФ shared host; this round is `$0`-oracle + ptxas-clean only. **GPU.md ┬з10 тЙе30 % box stays `[ ]` until this timed wall lands** (the structural advantage is proven; the timed flip needs the wall)

g3 caveats:
- The structural oracle counts launches + HBM C-write bytes тАФ a deterministic real measurement. It is NOT a timed wall; the timed perf advantage is the deferred follow-on
- The fused kernel is a one-thread-per-output naive GEMM (correctness + fusion-structure demonstration), not a WMMA-tiled perf kernel тАФ the fusion *advantage* (1 vs 3 launches, 1├Ч vs 3├Ч HBM C-write) is independent of the inner GEMM tiling
- cuBLAS-LT *does* have a limited `GELU_BIAS` epilogue; the baseline models the canonical NN-stack path using plain `cublasSgemm`/`cublasGemmEx` (no fused epilogue), which is what flame/PyTorch-eager-class stacks emit
- No LLVM (@F f1), no C-transpile change (@F f2) тАФ CPU codegen byte-identical pre/post (only doc + new artifact/tool files added)

### 1h тАФ F-FUSION-LAUNCH-AMORT тАФ launch-overhead amortization $0 oracle (2026-05-25) ЁЯЫ╕

The ┬з5f launch-overhead-amortization case made concrete + ptxas-clean. A single fused hexa-emitted kernel computes the **5-op elementwise chain `y = residual + scale * GeLU(a*x + b)`** (mul ┬╖ add ┬╖ gelu ┬╖ mul-by-scale ┬╖ add-residual) in ONE launch, with t1..t4 living in registers; a per-op baseline issues the SAME chain as **5 separate kernel launches**, each round-tripping the working tensor through HBM (eager-stack / per-op-library semantics). Pre-registered falsifier **F-FUSION-LAUNCH-AMORT**: the fused single-launch kernel beats the 5-launch baseline by тЙе30% wall in the launch-bound regime. This cycle is the **$0 structural/projection oracle + ptxas-clean**; the timed silicon wall is DEFERRED-to-serial (ubu-2 shared). Artifact: `archive/fires/gpu_fusion_launch_amort_2026_05_25/`.

- [x] **F-FUSION-LAUNCH-AMORT structural advantage PROVEN ($0 oracle, exit 0)** ЁЯЫ╕ тАФ deterministic hexa-native oracle (`oracle.hexa`, built native, exit 0). **Launch count: fused 1 vs baseline 5 (5.0├Ч fewer)**. **HBM traffic/elem: fused 2R+1W=3 vs baseline 6R+5W=11 (3.67├Ч more for baseline)**. **Closed-form wall projection** from MEASURED per-launch overhead (┬з1g F-RFC067-PB-TIMING, warm Nth-launch L=1 ┬╡s; conservative effective BW=200 GB/s): `wall_fused = L + Rf┬╖c┬╖n`, `wall_baseline = 5L + Rb┬╖c┬╖n`. Launch-bound (nтЖТ0): `pct_faster тЖТ 1 тИТ 1/5 = 80%`. Bandwidth-bound (nтЖТтИЮ): `pct_faster тЖТ 1 тИТ Rf/Rb = 1 тИТ 3/11 = 72.7%`. **The 30%-crossover `n* = 2.5L/(c┬╖(Rf тИТ 0.70┬╖Rb))` has `(Rf тИТ 0.70┬╖Rb) = (3 тИТ 7.7) = тИТ4.7 < 0` тЗТ n\* NEGATIVE тЗТ no crossover тЗТ the тЙе30% advantage is UNCONDITIONAL across all n**. Sample curve: n=64 тЖТ 79.98% ┬╖ n=1024 тЖТ 79.69% ┬╖ n=65536 тЖТ 74.6% ┬╖ n=1M тЖТ 72.88%. **The falsifier is over-satisfied** тАФ it predicted a launch-bound-only crossover, but the fused kernel wins on BOTH the launch axis (1<5) AND the HBM-traffic axis (3<11), so the тЙе30% wall win never drops below 30%. Verdict verbatim: `.verdicts/fusion-launch-amort/fusion_launch_amort.txt`.
- [x] **ptxas-clean тАФ `ptxas -arch=sm_80 -v` on ubu-2 (CUDA 12.0)** тАФ both PTX modules assemble clean, 0 spill. **fused_chain.ptx rc=0** (11 regs, 392 B cmem[0], 0 spill). **baseline_chain.ptx rc=0** (5 entries k1_mul/k2_add/k3_gelu/k4_mul_scale/k5_add_resid = 10/10/11/10/12 regs, all 0 spill). Pure ASCII (driver-JIT ptxas rejects non-ASCII PTX comments). Log: `archive/fires/gpu_fusion_launch_amort_2026_05_25/ptxas_clean.log`. ptxas is not a timed run (no GPU contention).
- [x] **numeric correctness harness** тАФ `host_fusion_launch.c` (cuLaunchKernel + cuEvent timing, `tool/r067_p4_host.c` pattern) compares the fused kernel to an f64 CPU reference of the identical chain (tanh-approx GeLU), tol 1e-2 abs (tanh.approx.f32 ~2тБ╗┬╣┬╣ rel bound). Numeric PASS confirmation is part of the DEFERRED timed fire.
- [x] **TIMED SILICON WALL тАФ CONFIRMED 2026-05-25** ЁЯЫ╕ЁЯЫ╕ тАФ `host_fusion_launch.c` fired on ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120 (GPU 0% util pre-fire, uncontended, 20 warmup + 200 timed median) across nтИИ{1024, 16384, 262144, 4194304, 16777216}: fused beats the 5-launch baseline **73.1тАУ76.2% wall UNCONDITIONALLY** тАФ n=1024 74.1%/3.86├Ч ┬╖ n=16384 73.1%/3.72├Ч ┬╖ n=262144 76.2%/4.20├Ч ┬╖ n=4194304 74.6%/3.93├Ч ┬╖ n=16.7M 73.5%/3.77├Ч, all тЙе30% gate PASS, numeric max|╬Ф|=1.1e-5 (abs) PASS. **The closed-form projection [72.7%,80%] is CONFIRMED BY MEASUREMENT** (ЁЯЯв SUPPORTED-NUMERICAL). **This FLIPS the ┬з10 "тЙе30% whole-program fusion advantage" box to `[x]`** (domain @goal ┬╖ ┬з5f launch-overhead axis). Verdict verbatim: `.verdicts/fusion-launch-amort-wall/F-FUSION-LAUNCH-AMORT-WALL.txt`.

g3 caveats:
- The 80% / 72.7% figures are a closed-form PROJECTION from a measured per-launch constant (L=1 ┬╡s) + a model (memory-bound elementwise; per-op kernel = bandwidth-limited) тАФ NOT a measured wall. The serial timed fire is the empirical confirmation.
- The HBM-traffic count (3 vs 11) is the structural ground truth; it is exact, not modeled. The launch-count (1 vs 5) is exact. The PROJECTION layer (translating those into a тЙе30% wall) is what the timed fire validates.
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). CPU codegen untouched.

### 1i тАФ F-FUSION-ATTN-WMMA тАФ Tensor-Core fused flash-attention codegen (round 2 of 3) (2026-05-25) ЁЯЫ╕

The Tensor-Core successor to the round-1 naive-scalar flash-attention kernel (┬з13 / `archive/fires/fusion_attention_flash_2026_05_25/`), which lost its wall **1.4тАУ1.5├Ч slower** than cuBLAS because its inner QK^T and ┬╖V GEMMs were scalar `fma` loops. This round re-authors the fused `softmax(QK^T/тИЪd)┬╖V` kernel with **both inner GEMMs on Tensor Cores** via `wmma.mma.sync m16n16k16` (f16 mul, f32 acc), the **S tile resident in SHARED MEMORY (never to HBM)**, and online softmax (running max + sum) on the smem S tile. Pre-registered falsifier **F-FUSION-ATTN-WMMA-WALL**: clause (a) ptxas-clean + 1 launch + 0 S-HBM + Tensor-Core inner GEMMs; clause (b) [ROUND 3] beats cuBLAS-batched-TC-GEMM+softmax by тЙе30% wall. **THIS round = codegen + ptxas-clean (3 arches) + $0 structural oracle (clause a); the timed wall (clause b) is DEFERRED-to-round-3** (parent runs timed fires serially тАФ uncontended GPU). Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_attention_wmma_2026_05_25/`.

- [x] **clause (a) тАФ WMMA fused kernel EMITS + ptxas-clean (3 arches)** ЁЯЫ╕ тАФ hand-emit `flash_attn_wmma.ptx` (RFC 067 WMMA cookbook + `compiler/codegen/nvptx_target.hexa::_nvptx_wmma_mnemonic` emit family). Pure ASCII (0 non-ascii bytes). **ptxas `-arch=sm_80` rc=0** (48 regs, 5824 B smem, 0 spill, 392 B cmem) ┬╖ **ptxas `-arch=sm_90` rc=0** (48 regs, 5824 B smem, 0 spill) ┬╖ **driver-JIT `sm_120` rc=0** on the live RTX 5070 (`cuModuleLoadDataEx` + `CU_JIT_TARGET_FROM_CUCONTEXT`, entry `flash_attn_wmma` resolved 48 regs / 5824 B static smem тАФ a LOAD probe, NO kernel launch, NO timing). **Footprint fits the RTX 5070 envelope** (┬з1f caps): 48 regs тЙк 65536/block, 5824 B smem = 11.8% of the 49152 B/block cap; S tile (1024 B) + O tile (4096 B) resident in smem.
- [x] **clause (a) тАФ structural moat PRESERVED + Tensor-Core inner GEMMs confirmed** ЁЯЫ╕ тАФ `$0` compiled-hexa oracle (`structural_oracle.hexa`, `hexa build` + run тАФ `hexa verify` g5 is broken on both ubu hosts, so compiled-hexa per the round protocol; stdout verbatim in verdict): **1 launch vs baseline 3**, **0 S-HBM vs baseline 4┬╖N┬▓┬╖4 B** (67 108 864 B @ N=2048), total-HBM ratio `R(N,d)=1.25+N/d` reproduced (4├ЧR(2048,64)=133). **Static PTX ground-truth grep**: `wmma.mma.sync` **├Ч5 distinct** (1├Ч `mma.row.col` QK^T + 4├Ч `mma.row.row` P┬╖V over d=64) **vs round-1 ZERO** тАФ the round-1 wall-loss root cause (scalar inner GEMMs) is ADDRESSED. **`st.global` ├Ч1** тАФ the ONLY HBM write is the final O; the S tile uses `wmma.store.d тАжshared.f32` exclusively тЗТ **S never touches HBM**.
- [x] **clause (b) ROUND-3 harness READY (NOT run)** тАФ `fa_wmma_host.c` (fused launcher: IEEE f16 in/out, f64 CPU reference on the f16-rounded inputs, rel-err тЙд 1e-2, `cuEvent` 20 warmup + 200 timed median) + `fa_cublas_tc_baseline.c` (cuBLAS `CUBLAS_GEMM_DEFAULT_TENSOR_OP` 3-launch QK^T тЖТ softmax kernel тЖТ P┬╖V, `cuEvent` timed). Both **`nvcc -c` compile-clean on ubu-2** (rc=0). Round-3 plan: serial uncontended fire at NтИИ{512,1024,2048,4096} d=64; win = `baseline_ms/fused_ms тЙе 1.30`.

g3 caveats:
- **WALL clause (b) тАФ ROUND-3 FIRED 2026-05-25: ЁЯФ┤ FALSIFIED.** Timed on ubu-2 RTX 5070 (uncontended, GPU 0% pre-fire, 20 warmup + 200 timed median, d=64): the fused single-CTA wmma kernel is **9.4тАУ15.5├Ч SLOWER** than the cuBLAS-TC 3-launch baseline тАФ N=512 0.157 vs 0.0166 ms (9.4├Ч) ┬╖ N=1024 0.335 vs 0.0309 ms (10.8├Ч) ┬╖ N=2048 0.819 vs 0.0617 ms (13.3├Ч) ┬╖ N=4096 2.930 vs 0.189 ms (15.5├Ч) тАФ **AND numeric FAILs** (max_rel 2.6тАУ4.8 > 1e-2 tol; max_abs ~3тАУ6e-5). **Ruled-out axis (the round-3 finding):** Tensor-Core *instructions* alone do NOT win the wall. The round-2 kernel is **single-CTA** (S/P/O tiles + 48 regs resident in one block's smem) so it occupies **~1 of the RTX 5070's 48 SMs** while cuBLAS launches a grid of thousands of CTAs тАФ the structural moat (1 launch, 0 S-HBM) is real but dominated by a 47/48-SMs-idle parallelism deficit. Beating cuBLAS attention requires cuBLAS-grade **multi-CTA work distribution + occupancy + tiling** (flash-attention's actual design: one CTA per (query-block, head)), not just `wmma.mma.sync`. The clause-(a) verdict (ЁЯФ╡ codegen/structural) stands; clause (b) is a closed-negative. Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-attention-wmma-wall/F-FUSION-ATTN-WMMA-WALL.txt`.
- **┬з10 box is NOT touched.** The "тЙе30% whole-program fusion" box is already `[x]` (flipped via the ┬з5f launch-amortization axis, PR #1028). This GEMM-fusion (attention) axis needs its OWN round-3 timed Tensor-Core wall to win тАФ flipping nothing here.
- The kernel keeps the S tile in shared memory and applies online softmax via a shared-mem round-trip of the S/O tiles (correct-by-construction, sidesteps the mma fragment laneтЖТ(row,col) layout) тАФ a perf-relevant choice the round-3 fire measures; an in-fragment softmax is a follow-on optimization if the wall is close.
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). `compiler/codegen/*.hexa` UNTOUCHED (hand-emit PTX); CPU codegen MD5 preserved (`x86_64_linux.hexa b50a2a3cтАж`, `arm64_darwin.hexa b0a397dcтАж`).

### 1j тАФ F-FUSION-ATTN-MULTICTA тАФ multi-CTA wide-KV fused flash-attention (round 4) (2026-05-25) ЁЯЯа

The round-4 attack on the GEMM-fusion (attention) axis after round-3's ЁЯФ┤ wall loss. Pre-registered falsifier **F-FUSION-ATTN-MULTICTA-WALL**: author a **CORRECT, multi-CTA** fused flash-attention kernel that saturates the SMs (keeping online softmax + S-in-shared-never-HBM + wmma inner GEMMs), then re-time vs cuBLAS-TC 3-launch тАФ win = тЙе30% faster (ratio тЙд 0.70). **Result: ЁЯЯа QUANTIFIED-PARTIAL** тАФ a correct multi-CTA kernel that closes the gap ~3тАУ8├Ч but does **not** beat cuBLAS-TC. Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_attention_multicta_2026_05_25/`.

- [x] **NUMERIC тАФ round-3 "FAIL" was a METRIC ARTIFACT, kernel is CORRECT** ЁЯЯв тАФ round 3's reported `max_rel 2.6тАУ4.8 = FAIL` came from the naive `|err|/(|want|+1e-6)` metric exploding on the **many near-zero attention output elements** (|want| тЙк 1e-6) тАФ NOT a kernel bug. Under the honest **per-row-scaled + RMS** relative metric the round-3 *algorithm* is already correct, proven independently in clean CUDA-C `nvcuda::wmma` (rel_rowscale 5e-4, rms 2.6e-4, PASS). The shipped hand-PTX multi-CTA kernel `flash_attn_wmma_mcta` then PASSes numeric at all 4 shapes vs the f64 CPU ref: rel_rowscale **6.3e-4 / 5.6e-4 / 6.3e-4 / 7.1e-4** (N=512/1024/2048/4096), rms ~2.7e-4 тАФ matching the CUDA-C oracle exactly (тЗТ the hand-PTX WMMA fragment handling is correct).
- [x] **round-3 was ALSO already multi-CTA** тАФ the round-3 grid was `N/16` CTAs (not single-CTA); the real deficit was **1 warp/CTA doing per-16-key serial online-softmax overhead**. The round-4 lever is **widening the KV tile from BK=16 to BK=256** (16 wmma key-subtiles per softmax round), amortizing the softmax+rescale overhead 16├Ч.
- [x] **ptxas-clean (3 arches) + footprint** тАФ pure ASCII (0 non-ascii bytes). **sm_80 rc=0** (41 regs, 28864 B smem, 0 spill, 392 B cmem) ┬╖ **sm_90 rc=0** (32 regs, 28864 B smem, 0 spill) ┬╖ **driver-JIT sm_120** loads + runs OK. 28864 B smem/CTA = **58.7% of the 49152 B/block cap (FITS)**; S(16├Ч256)+O(16├Ч64) resident in smem, never to HBM. **Grid occupancy:** `N/16` тЗТ **32 / 64 / 128 / 256 CTAs** (vs 48 SMs) тАФ max grid saturation (multi-warp-per-CTA was MEASURED slower: cuts grid count + raises smem/CTA).
- [x] **TIMED WALL (clause b) тАФ ЁЯЯа PARTIAL** тАФ ubu-2 RTX 5070 (clean, 0% util, 0 compute procs, cuEvent 20 warmup + 200 timed median, d=64). Shipped **hand-PTX fused vs cuBLAS-TC**: N=512 0.0566 vs 0.0167 ms (**3.40├Ч**) ┬╖ N=1024 0.114 vs 0.0308 ms (**3.70├Ч**) ┬╖ N=2048 0.244 vs 0.0617 ms (**3.96├Ч**) ┬╖ N=4096 0.954 vs 0.190 ms (**5.01├Ч**). **Gap closure: round-3 9.4тАУ15.5├Ч тЖТ round-4 3.4тАУ5.0├Ч.** The CUDA-C-validated geometry floor (nvcc-vectorized scalar loops) is even tighter: **1.32 / 1.44 / 1.65 / 2.04├Ч** тАФ the hand-PTX scalar softmax/rescale loops are un-vectorized (~2тАУ2.5├Ч slower than nvcc's `ld.shared.v4`/unroll), so a hexa-codegen path with vectorized smem loads could approach this floor.

g3 caveats:
- **NOT a win.** Fused is still **1.3тАУ5.0├Ч slower** than cuBLAS-TC (ratio > 0.70) тАФ the тЙе30% GEMM-fusion-axis win is **not achieved**. Honest tier = ЁЯЯа.
- **Binding constraint identified:** at d=64 the **per-16├Ч16-tile online-softmax overhead тАФ NOT S-HBM traffic тАФ is the wall**. cuBLAS amortizes its GEMMs over huge tiles the tiny 16├Ч16 WMMA fused path cannot match; wide-KV amortization narrows but does not close this. The structural moat (1 launch, 0 S-HBM) is real and preserved but not the bottleneck at this shape.
- **┬з10 box is NOT touched** тАФ stays `[x]` only via the launch-amort axis (PR #1028). The GEMM-fusion (attention) axis remains NOT-won.
- **No paper** тАФ `paper_gate` forbids ЁЯЯа partial sections; this is neither a тЙе30% win nor a clean closed-negative (the kernel works, it just loses the wall).
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). `compiler/codegen/*.hexa` UNTOUCHED (hand-emit PTX); the CUDA-C `.cu` files are correctness/geometry oracles only, not the shipped fused path. CPU codegen MD5 preserved.

### 1k тАФ F-FUSION-ATTN-DECOMP тАФ full dimensional-decomposition sweep ┬╖ KV-split hypothesis (round 5) (2026-05-25) ЁЯЯатЖТclosed-neg

The round-5 attack: map the **complete parallel-decomposition space** of the fused `softmax(QK^T/тИЪd)┬╖V` kernel vs cuBLAS-TC 3-launch, and specifically test whether the **KV-SPLIT (z-axis, flash-decoding)** dimension closes the small-N occupancy gap left by round-4 (N=512 grid = only 32 CTAs < 48 SMs). Pre-registered falsifier **F-FUSION-ATTN-DECOMP-WALL**. Swept **153 configs** = N{512,1024,2048,4096} ├Ч Bq{16,32,64} ├Ч kv_split{1,2,4,8,16} ├Ч BK{64,128,256}, d=64 тАФ **all numeric PASS** (rel_rowscale тЙд 1e-2 vs f64 CPU ref). Tool: a CUDA-C `nvcuda::wmma` **flash-decoding oracle** (2-kernel: partial-O + LSE-merge), authored correctly тАФ `kv_split=1` reduces EXACTLY to the round-4 algorithm (max_abs 4.02796e-05 identical). **Result: ЁЯЯа QUANTIFIED-PARTIAL тЖТ closed-negative.** Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_attention_decomp_2026_05_25/`; ledger `exports/sweep/gpu-attn-decomp-2026-05-25/`.

- [x] **KV-SPLIT CLOSES the small-N occupancy gap тАФ user hypothesis CONFIRMED** ЁЯЯв тАФ N=512 Bq16: occupancy **32 тЖТ 128 CTAs** (kv=1тЖТkv=4), wall **0.146 тЖТ 0.058 ms** = **2.53├Ч intra-framework speedup**, reaching **parity with the round-4 single-kernel** (0.0568 ms) despite the 2-pass partial-O+merge tax. The benefit **saturates** at the split K where ctas_partial тЙе ~48 SMs (N=512 plateaus at kv=4=128 CTAs; **kv=8/16 REGRESS** via over-subscription + merge cost).
- [x] **KV-split is a SMALL-N-ONLY lever** тАФ at NтЙе2048 the grid is already saturated by `N/Bq` alone, so KV-split adds only the partial-O HBM round-trip tax (grows O(N┬╖split┬╖d)): decomp-best **0.668 ms vs round-4 single-kernel 0.245 ms @ N=2048 (2.7├Ч WORSE)**. Net-neutral at small N, net-negative at large N.
- [x] **BK=256 confirmed best** within every fixed (N,Bq,kv) (round-4 finding re-confirmed); **Bq>16 uniformly slower** (cuts grid, the opposite of what small-N needs).
- [x] **OPTIMUM PER SHAPE (vs cuBLAS-TC)** тАФ N=512 Bq16/kv4/BK128 **3.47├Ч** ┬╖ N=1024 Bq32/kv4/BK256 **5.88├Ч** ┬╖ N=2048 Bq64/kv4/BK256 **10.82├Ч** ┬╖ N=4096 Bq16/kv8/BK256 **13.17├Ч**. Best overall = **3.47├Ч @ N=512**.

g3 caveats:
- **NOT a win.** Best ratio 3.47├Ч (> 0.70). The тЙе30% GEMM-fusion-axis win is **not achieved** by any decomposition. Honest tier = ЁЯЯа.
- **Closed-negative on the decomposition axis:** *no dimensional decomposition of hand-PTX flash-attn beats cuBLAS-TC at d=64.* KV-split trades **occupancy тЖФ HBM-traffic** тАФ it does not breach the round-4 binding constraint (per-16├Ч16-tile online-softmax overhead vs cuBLAS huge-tile GEMM efficiency). The GEMM-tile-efficiency wall is **confirmed fundamental**.
- The 2-pass oracle's absolute walls carry a partial-O HBM round-trip + 2nd-launch tax the round-4 single-kernel avoids; the **decomposition trend** is isolated within the consistent 2-pass frame, with the round-4 single-kernel given as the absolute cross-reference.
- **┬з10 box is NOT touched** тАФ stays `[x]` via launch-amort only; GEMM-fusion (attention) axis remains NOT-won.
- **No paper.** Captured as a closed-negative finding in the discovery log + ledger; `paper_gate` not triggered (no тЙе30% win; the closed-negative is a re-confirmation of the round-4 wall via a new axis, not a fresh disproof worth a paper scaffold).
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). `compiler/codegen/*.hexa` UNTOUCHED (hand-emit PTX path); the CUDA-C `.cu` is a correctness/decomposition oracle only. CPU codegen MD5 preserved.

### 1m тАФ F-FUSION-ATTN-ROOFLINE тАФ N204 roofline-GEMM-toolkit transplant (round 7) (2026-05-25) ЁЯЯатЖТclosed-neg

The round-7 attack: hexa ALREADY hits the GEMM roofline standalone (N204 "TMA SWIZZLE_128B" reached **cuBLAS 0.978 parity @ M=8192**, PRs #333/#335) тАФ the round-4/5 fused attention lost its wall (best 3.47├Ч) NOT because hexa can't do roofline GEMM, but because the fused kernel's inner QK^T and P┬╖V GEMMs were naive (single-warp, 16├Ч16 wmma tiles, no TMA, no double-buffer, no swizzle). This round transplants the proven N204 roofline toolkit (TMA `cp.async.bulk.tensor` + double-buffered K/V tiles + 64├Ч64 large `mma.sync.m16n8k16` tiles + 4-warp 2├Ч2 layout) into the fused `softmax(QK^T/тИЪd)┬╖V` inner GEMMs and measures % of the cuBLAS-TC + theoretical roofline. Pre-registered falsifier **F-FUSION-ATTN-ROOFLINE**: ratio тЙд 1.10 vs cuBLAS-TC on at least one shape (NтИИ{2048,4096}, d=64) AND report achieved % of the sm_120 FP16 tensor-core roofline. **Result: ЁЯЯа INSUFFICIENT (target NOT hit) + closed-negative finding.** Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_attention_roofline_2026_05_25/`.

- [x] **clause (a) тАФ kernel emits + ptxas-clean** ЁЯЫ╕ тАФ hand-emit `flash_attn_tma_v2_{2048,4096}.ptx` (pure ASCII, 0 non-ascii bytes). **ptxas `-arch=sm_120a` rc=0** (68 regs, 0 spills, 1 barrier, 8 B stack). 5 `cp.async.bulk.tensor` (TMA) + 64 `mma.sync.aligned.m16n8k16` + 32 `ldmatrix` + 1 `st.global` (final O only тАФ S NEVER to HBM, moat preserved). cuOccupancyMaxActiveBlocksPerMultiprocessor = **1 CTA/SM** (smem 99136 B vs optin/SM 102400 B).
- [x] **clause (b) тАФ NUMERIC PASS via fa_mma_oracle.cu + silicon fire** ЁЯЯв тАФ both shapes pass the honest per-row-scaled metric: N=2048 rel_rowscale 6.11e-4 / rms_rel 2.72e-4 ┬╖ N=4096 rel_rowscale 7.14e-4 / rms_rel 2.72e-4. Matches the round-4 oracle EXACTLY (max_abs 3.11e-5 @ N=4096 identical) тЖТ algorithmic equivalence confirmed.
- [x] **ЁЯЫ╕ MMA-FRAGMENT-MAP DISCOVERY** ЁЯЯв тАФ the round-7 probe campaign (`probe2.cu` + `probe3.cu`) empirically established that **`mma.sync.m16n8k16 .trans` + `ldmatrix.x4` performs an 8├Ч8-BLOCK transpose within each 16├Ч16 fragment, NOT a full 16├Ч16 transpose**. Non-trans + `mma.row.col` gives `C = A┬╖B^T` (err 1e-7 MATCH). The P┬╖V GEMM (contraction along V rows) therefore CANNOT use the same `.trans`-B path as QK^T; **v2 pre-transposes V into a separate smem buffer** so the proven non-trans path drives both GEMMs (probe3 err 6e-8 MATCH). Non-obvious empirical fact about m16n8k16 ldmatrix.x4 semantics not surfaced by PTX ISA narrative reading.
- [x] **ЁЯФ┤ clause (c) тАФ TIMED WALL ratio NOT тЙд1.10** тАФ fired on ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120, GPU 0% util, 0 compute procs (uncontended). 20 warmup + 200 timed cuEvent median:
  - **N=2048**: fused **0.324864 ms** / cuBLAS-TC **0.061568 ms** тЖТ **ratio 5.276├Ч SLOWER**. Fused 3.31 TFLOPS ┬╖ cuBLAS 17.44 TFLOPS.
  - **N=4096**: fused **1.281312 ms** / cuBLAS-TC **0.186624 ms** тЖТ **ratio 6.866├Ч SLOWER**. Fused 3.35 TFLOPS ┬╖ cuBLAS 23.01 TFLOPS.
- [x] **% OF ROOFLINE** (stated assumptions: sm_120 RTX 5070 from ┬з1f caps тАФ 48 SM ┬╖ 2.542 GHz ┬╖ 192-bit bus):
  - **% of cuBLAS HGEMM achievable ceiling (~70.2 TFLOPS @ N204 M=8192)**: N=2048 **4.71%** ┬╖ N=4096 **4.77%**.
  - **% of theoretical FP16-TC peak (48 SM ├Ч 4 TC ├Ч 256 FMA ├Ч 2 FLOP ├Ч 2.542 GHz = 249.9 TFLOPS)**: N=2048 **1.32%** ┬╖ N=4096 **1.34%**.
  - cuBLAS-TC 3-launch attention reaches 17.4 / 23.0 TFLOPS = 24.8% / 32.8% of its own HGEMM ceiling тАФ so cuBLAS's attention itself is ~3-4├Ч off roofline.
- [x] **GAP-CLOSURE TRAJECTORY (final)** тАФ round-3 9.4-15.5├Ч тЖТ round-4 3.4-5.0├Ч тЖТ round-5 3.47├Ч тЖТ **ROUND-7 5.3-6.9├Ч (REGRESSION)**.
- [x] **OCCUPANCY ATTRIBUTION (direct measurement)** тАФ `cuOccupancyMaxActiveBlocksPerMultiprocessor` on the real fn returned **1 CTA/SM** (smem-bound). At N=2048 grid=32 CTAs тЖТ **only 32 of 48 SMs populated (66.7% SM coverage)**. At N=4096 grid=64 тЖТ 48 SMs 1-CTA + 16 CTAs queued for serialized second wave. Round-4's BM=16 kernel had **8 CTAs/SM**; the 64├Ч64 attention tile multiplies the resident-set smem 8├Ч (Q + K[2] + V[2] + V^T[2] + S + P + O all simultaneously) тЖТ occupancy collapse.
- [x] **DOUBLE-BUFFER ATTRIBUTION (paired-shape A/B)** тАФ single-buffer occupancy-test variant (`flash_attn_tma_sb`, smem 74560 B, same 1 CTA/SM): wall 0.324896 ms. v2 double-buffer: 0.324864 ms. **╬Ф 0.01% тАФ double-buffer ZERO BENEFIT here**: kernel is occupancy-bound, not DMA-bound; the TMA overlap opportunity is unrealized (no parallel compute to hide loads behind at 1 CTA/SM, only 4 warps with mma chain that can't overlap its own smem dependencies on the same slot).

g3 caveats:
- **NOT a win.** Best ratio 5.27├Ч (> 1.10 by 4.8├Ч). Pre-registered target NOT hit. Honest tier = ЁЯЯа INSUFFICIENT + closed-negative finding on the technique axis.
- **CLOSED-NEGATIVE (terminal):** *the N204 standalone-GEMM roofline toolkit DOES NOT TRANSPLANT to fused flash-attention.* The 64├Ч64 tile that buys roofline-GEMM performance for a standalone GEMM COSTS attention occupancy because fused attention has fundamentally different smem residency (Q + K + V + V^T + S + P + O simultaneously resident тАФ multiple O(BM ├Ч BK) and O(BM ├Ч d) tiles). The technique is correct in isolation (numeric PASS, ptxas-clean) but the architectural fit is wrong for this kernel. **Which N204 technique helped most: NONE moved the wall positively.** Rank by attribution: 64├Ч64 tile (BACKFIRED, the main regressor) > TMA loads (NEUTRAL, save HBM but no occupancy to absorb) > double-buffer (ZERO) > swizzle (NOT APPLIED in v2 because the .trans-B path is invalid for P┬╖V).
- **┬з10 box is NOT touched** тАФ stays `[x]` via launch-amort only; GEMM-fusion (attention) axis remains NOT-won.
- **No paper.** ORANGE INSUFFICIENT + re-confirmation of an already-CLOSED-NEGATIVE wall via a new failed-axis тАФ `paper_gate` forbids per project.tape `paper_significance`.
- **Next-round wedge (recommendation):** shallower tile BM=32 (or BM=16 with multi-warp) + REGISTER-RESIDENT O (acc in registers, not smem) + selective TMA to restore тЙе2-4 CTAs/SM occupancy WITHOUT abandoning TMA loads. Smem budget then ~34-50 KB тЖТ 2 CTAs/SM, doubling occupancy.
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). `compiler/codegen/*.hexa` UNTOUCHED (hand-emit PTX path); `.cu`/`.c` are oracle/host only. CPU codegen MD5 preserved.

### 1n тАФ F-FUSION-ATTN-MULTIWARP тАФ multi-warp BM=64 + cp.async K/V double-buffer (round 10, campaign capstone attempt) (2026-05-26) ЁЯЯа

The round-10 attack on the GEMM-fusion (attention) axis-A, taking R9's (#1121) next-wedge prescription literally. R9 diagnosed the d=64 16├Ч16 **single-warp** tile as **latency/dependency-bound** (occupancy was plenty at 24-28 CTAs/SM): the per-tile row-reduction between the QK^T mma and the P┬╖V mma sits on the critical path with no other warp's work to hide it. R10 breaks that floor two ways on the R9 reg-S + smem-scratch-reduce base (NOT warp-shuffle тАФ R9 closed-negatived that): **(1) multi-warp BM=64** тАФ 4 warps/CTA (block=128), each owning 16 *independent* query rows (warp w тЖТ rows [w┬╖16..w┬╖16+15], no cross-warp softmax), the 4 warps **sharing one K/V smem tile** (loaded once per CTA тЖТ no HBM-traffic multiplication); **(2) cp.async.cg K/V double-buffer** тАФ the next K/V tile prefetches async while the current tile computes, overlapping HBM load latency with the mma pipeline. Pre-registered falsifier **F-FUSION-ATTN-MULTIWARP**: numeric PASS + ptxas-clean + beats cuBLAS-stack (`fused_ms < cublas_stack_ms`) on тЙе1 (N,d) shape, d=64. **Result: ЁЯЯа INSUFFICIENT (best-of-campaign, does NOT cross 1.0├Ч).** Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_attn_multiwarp_2026_05_26/`.
- [x] **NUMERIC тАФ all 4 shapes PASS** ЁЯЯв тАФ `fa_mw_cpasync` vs f64 CPU ref + NaN/Inf hard-fail counter: rel_rowscale **5.41e-4 / 5.67e-4 / 6.11e-4 / 7.14e-4** (N=512/1024/2048/4096), naninf=**0**, bit-equivalent in tolerance to R8/R9. ptxas-clean 0-spill sm_80 (91 reg) / sm_90a (93 reg) / sm_90 (93 reg); **14336 B smem тЙк 49152 B cap** (double-buffer K/V 8192 B + per-warp scratch). Occupancy reg-bound at **5 CTAs/SM ├Ч 4 warps = 20 warps/SM** (vs R9 25 warps/SM single-warp тЖТ occupancy still NOT binding).
- **WALL тАФ ЁЯФ┤ FALSIFIED as a WIN / ЁЯЯа best-of-campaign gap-closure.** cuEvent 20 warmup + 200 timed median, ubu-2 RTX 5070 (0% util pre-fire, ~0.4% repro): ratio vs cuBLAS-stack **1.613├Ч / 1.309├Ч / 1.186├Ч / 1.149├Ч** @ N=512/1024/2048/4096 тАФ best **1.149├Ч @ N=4096** (14.9% BELOW cuBLAS). Does NOT cross 1.0├Ч on any shape тЖТ the pre-registered win condition is NOT met. **Gap-closure: R9 best 1.662├Ч (same session) тЖТ R10 1.149├Ч;** R10 is **1.447├Ч FASTER than R9 single-warp** at N=4096 (0.2173 vs 0.3145 ms) тАФ the fastest fused attention of the whole campaign.
- **LEVER ISOLATION (controlled A/B тАФ `fa_mw_noasync` drops only cp.async, single-buffer synchronous load):** **cp.async double-buffer is the DOMINANT lever** тАФ mw+cpasync is **1.34├Ч / 1.46├Ч / 1.50├Ч / 1.40├Ч** faster than no-async multi-warp. The **multi-warp lever alone** (no-async vs R9) is **1.12├Ч / 1.28├Ч / 1.37├Ч / 1.04├Ч** тАФ real but smaller, and **fades to 1.04├Ч at N=4096**. BOTH levers moved it; overlapping the HBM K/V load with the mma pipeline closed most of the gap.
- **RESIDUAL BOTTLENECK:** still latency-bound, but the exposed latency moved from R9's per-tile row-reduction to (1) the intra-warp QK^T-mma тЖТ row-reduce тЖТ P┬╖V-mma dependency chain each warp still serializes, and (2) the per-K-tile `__syncthreads` barrier across the 4 warps sharing the double-buffered smem. At d=64 the wmma tile is only 4 d-tiles deep тЖТ arithmetic intensity too low to saturate the tensor cores vs cuBLAS's two big TC GEMMs; grid=N/64 also under-fills the 48 SMs at NтЙд2048. NOT bandwidth, NOT occupancy.
- **┬з10 box is NOT touched** тАФ stays `[x]` via launch-amort only; the GEMM-fusion (attention) axis-A remains NOT-won at d=64 (no 1.0├Ч cross). No new closure row flipped.
- **No paper.** ЁЯЯа INSUFFICIENT тАФ `paper_gate` / `paper_significance` (project.tape) forbid a paper without a terminal WIN; paper triggers only on a GREEN 1.0├Ч-cross capstone.
- **Next-round wedge (recommendation):** (a) **2-stage software COMPUTE pipeline** тАФ overlap the P┬╖V mma of K-tile j with the QK^T mma of tile j+1 to break the intra-warp 3-phase chain that is now the floor (cp.async already overlaps the LOAD; this overlaps the COMPUTE phases); (b) **head dim dтЙе128 sweep** тАФ cuBLAS's S=N├ЧN HBM round-trip cost is fixed but fused TC utilization rises with deeper d-tiles, so the fused path may favor larger d where R10's 4-d-tile arithmetic-intensity ceiling lifts; (c) **wgmma** (sm_90 async warpgroup mma) for higher per-instruction TC throughput. Do NOT retry warp-shuffle softmax (R9 closed-negative) nor expect multi-warp-alone to help at large N (R10 measured it fades to 1.04├Ч).
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). `compiler/codegen/*.hexa` UNTOUCHED (hand-emit PTX / CUDA-oracle path); `.cu`/`.c` are oracle/host only. CPU codegen MD5 preserved.

---

### 1o тАФ F-FUSION-ATTN-DSWEEP-PIPE тАФ head_dim sweep + 2-stage compute pipeline (round 11) (2026-05-26) ЁЯЯатЖТnear-ceiling-closed-neg

The round-11 attack taking R10's (#1135) two next-wedges literally тАФ two coupled probes on the GEMM-fusion (attention) axis-A. **(A) head_dim sweep:** parameterize R10's multi-warp BM=64 + cp.async kernel over head_dim `D` (`DTILES = D/16` d-tiles), fire at dтИИ{64,128,256} ├Ч NтИИ{1024,2048,4096}. Hypothesis: at dтЙе128 the fused inner-GEMM arithmetic intensity rises тЖТ the fused path may CROSS тЙд1.0├Ч (above cuBLAS-stack). **(B) 2-stage COMPUTE pipeline** at best-d: overlap the P┬╖V mma of K-tile j with the QK^T mma of tile j+1 (break the intra-warp dependency chain R10 found is now the floor тАФ distinct from cp.async which overlapped the LOAD). Pre-registered falsifier **F-FUSION-ATTN-DSWEEP-PIPE**: WIN = `fused_ms < cublas_stack_ms` (ratio тЙд1.0├Ч) on тЙе1 (N,d). **Result: ЁЯЯа NEAR-CEILING CLOSED-NEGATIVE тАФ BOTH levers FALSIFIED; the d-lever moves the WRONG way.** Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_attn_dsweep_pipe_2026_05_26/`.
- **BASELINE INTEGRITY (instrument-first, g3):** the fused kernel is FP16-Tensor-Core; the fair baseline is the FP16 cuBLAS-TC 3-launch stack. A launch-decomposition probe (`cublas_probe.cu`) caught that a NAIVE one-thread-per-row softmax was a **13├Ч SLOWER STRAWMAN** (softmax kernel alone 2.154 ms @ N=4096 d=64 vs the two GEMMs' 0.316 ms) тАФ a ЁЯЯв against it would have been **DISHONEST and was REJECTED.** Fixed to an OPTIMIZED block-per-row parallel-reduction softmax; corrected cuBLAS-TC = **0.176 ms @ N=4096 d=64**, matching R10's recorded 0.189 ms baseline. All ratios below use the fair baseline.
- [x] **NUMERIC тАФ all 12 measured shapes PASS** ЁЯЯв тАФ `fa_dsweep` per-row-scaled rel **5.6тАУ7.1e-4**, naninf=0 at all 9 (N,d); d=64 rows bit-identical to R10 (faithful parameterization). `fa_pipe` (probe B, d=64) PASS bit-identical to R10. ptxas-clean 0-spill: `fa_dsweep` sm_80 **91 / 148 / 247 reg**, smem **14336 / 22528 / 38912 B** @ d=64/128/256 (all тЙк 49152 B cap); `fa_pipe` 104 reg / 18432 B.
- **PROBE (A) WALL тАФ ЁЯФ┤ d-lever FALSIFIED IN THE WRONG DIRECTION.** ratio fused/cuBLAS-TC WORSENS monotonically with d: d=64 **{1.229, 1.225, 1.234}** ┬╖ d=128 **{2.149, 1.673, 1.752}** ┬╖ d=256 **{2.967, 2.290, 2.217}** @ N={1024,2048,4096}. Best ratio **1.225├Ч @ d=64 N=2048** never crosses тЙд1.0├Ч. **Root cause:** cuBLAS's two big TC GEMMs are dominated by the d-INDEPENDENT N├ЧN S HBM round-trip (cuBLAS @ N=4096 barely slows: 0.176 тЖТ 0.233 тЖТ 0.354 ms); the fused per-warp **serial d-tile loop** (`DTILES` mma + scale_o + P-repack on the critical chain) scales LINEARLY with d (0.217 тЖТ 0.409 тЖТ 0.786 ms). Raising head_dim **WIDENS** the gap тАФ the d-trend DIVERGES from a crossover. d-lever RULED OUT.
- **PROBE (B) WALL тАФ ЁЯФ┤ compute-pipeline FALSIFIED.** At best-d=64: v1 (hoist QK^T but serialize the load) = **+18.9..27.9% SLOWER** (confirms R10's cp.async LOAD-overlap is dominant тАФ do not trade it away). v2 (race-free **triple-buffer** K+V keeping 2-deep load overlap AND hoisting QK^T(j+1) from the prefetched slot, numeric bit-identical) = **+4.9 / +4.2 / +2.4% SLOWER** than R10 @ N=1024/2048/4096. The intra-warp QK^TтЖТreduceтЖТP┬╖V chain is **NOT an exposed pipeline bubble** тАФ with 4 warps ├Ч 20 warps/SM the scheduler already interleaves the independent wmma streams; the hoist's extra `__syncthreads` + register pressure (93тЖТ104) cost more than any gain. Campaign-best ratio stays R10's **1.149├Ч @ N=4096 d=64**.
- **┬з10 box is NOT touched** тАФ stays `[x]` via launch-amort only; the GEMM-fusion (attention) axis-A remains NOT-won at dтИИ{64..256} (no 1.0├Ч cross). The two most-plausible remaining levers (deeper d, compute-overlap) are now both RULED OUT тАФ the inner-GEMM TC-utilization gap is FUNDAMENTAL at these shapes. A valid g3 near-ceiling closed-negative.
- **No paper.** ЁЯЯа тАФ `paper_gate` / `paper_significance` (project.tape) forbid a paper without a terminal WIN; the closed-negative rules out two axes but is not a тЙд1.0├Ч capstone.
- **Next untried lever:** (a) **wgmma** (sm_90 async warpgroup mma m64nNk16) тАФ the ONE lever not yet tried that directly attacks the TC-utilization gap (bigger per-instruction tile тЖТ higher arithmetic intensity per issue); (b) **FP8 e4m3** on Blackwell TCs to double throughput; (c) accept fused attention at dтИИ{64..256} as a measured near-ceiling and pivot the fusable-axis @goal to an op-pair where cuBLAS truly forces an HBM round-trip AND the fused inner GEMM can saturate TCs. Do NOT re-sweep d (ruled out) nor re-pipeline the compute at d=64 (ruled out).
- No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). `compiler/codegen/*.hexa` UNTOUCHED; `.cu`/`.c` are oracle/host only. CPU codegen MD5 preserved.

### 1l тАФ F-FUSION-AXISA-BREADTH тАФ whole-program-fusion moat across the NN elementwise/norm surface (2026-05-25) ЁЯЫ╕ЁЯЫ╕

Broadens the ┬з10 moat (already `[x]` via the launch-amort wall, ┬з1h / PR #1028) from ONE workload to the **NN elementwise/reduction surface**: LayerNorm ┬╖ RMSNorm ┬╖ Softmax ┬╖ SwiGLU. Each = a fused 1-kernel vs an eager multi-launch baseline, timed on ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120 (uncontended 0% util, 20 warmup + 200 timed median), numeric vs an f64 CPU reference using the **HONEST per-row-scaled RMS rel metric** (tol 1e-2 тАФ avoids the round-3 attention near-zero false-FAIL). Pre-registered falsifier per workload: fused (1 launch) beats eager by тЙе30% wall. `hexa verify` (g5) is BROKEN on both ubu hosts тАФ correctness settled via the compiled f64-ref harness, stdout persisted verbatim.

- [x] **LayerNorm** ЁЯЯв тАФ eager 4-launch {reduce-mean, reduce-var, normalize, affine} тЖТ fused 1; launch 4├Ч, HBM 6тЖТ3. **large 4096├Ч4096 = 66.2%** (fused 0.232 ms vs eager 0.687 ms, 2.96├Ч) ┬╖ **small 256├Ч512 = 72.7%** (3.67├Ч). numeric rel тЙд 1.5e-7. Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-axisA-layernorm/`.
- [x] **RMSNorm (LLaMA)** ЁЯЯв тАФ eager 3-launch {reduce-sq, normalize, scale} тЖТ fused 1; launch 3├Ч, HBM 5тЖТ3. **large = 59.5%** (0.232 vs 0.573 ms, 2.47├Ч) ┬╖ **small = 58.6%** (2.41├Ч). numeric rel тЙд 1.4e-7. Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-axisA-rmsnorm/`.
- [x] **Softmax (online)** ЁЯЯв тАФ eager 4-launch {row-max, exp, row-sum, div} тЖТ fused 1; launch 4├Ч, HBM 6тЖТ4. **large = 65.9%** (0.238 vs 0.698 ms, 2.93├Ч) ┬╖ **small = 56.3%** (2.29├Ч). numeric rel тЙд 1.9e-7 (HONEST per-row RMS тАФ softmax probs go near zero). Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-axisA-softmax/`.
- [x] **SwiGLU** ЁЯЯв тАФ eager 3-launch {sigmoid, mul-gate, mul-up} тЖТ fused 1; launch 3├Ч, HBM 8тЖТ3 (largest traffic cut тАФ eager materialises s and t in HBM). **large n=16.78M = 63.0%** (0.334 vs 0.903 ms, 2.70├Ч) ┬╖ **small n=131072 = 47.8%** (1.92├Ч). numeric rel тЙд 3.4e-7. Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-axisA-swiglu/`.

**4/4 workloads PASS тЙе30% in BOTH launch-bound and bandwidth-bound regimes (8/8 measurements, 8/8 numeric).** The moat is now a robust GENERAL result across **N+1 = 5 workloads** (these 4 + launch-amort 73тАУ76%), not a single data point. cuBLAS/cuDNN supply tuned GEMMs but the elementwise/norm/activation glue is exactly what fusion owns. All ptxas modules `-arch=sm_90 -v` clean, 0 spill. Ledger `exports/sweep/gpu-axisA-breadth-2026-05-25/`; artifact `archive/fires/fusion_axisA_breadth_2026_05_25/`. No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). CPU codegen untouched (hand-emit PTX, pure ASCII).

### 1n тАФ Axis E тАФ autoregressive single-token fusion (LLM decode) тАФ round 8 of N ┬╖ structural + projection (2026-05-25) ЁЯЫ╕ЁЯЫ╕ЁЯЫ╕

Novel axis E (sibling to axes A/B/C/D), declared post-axis-C. Fuses an entire transformer-decoder layer step at autoregressive batch=1 (post-first-token) decode into **2 mega-kernels per layer** (`decode_attn_fused` + `decode_ffn_fused`) so the q-vector flows through registers/smem across all 17+ logical ops (LN ┬╖ 3-GEMV Q/K/V ┬╖ KV-append ┬╖ QK ┬╖ softmax ┬╖ PV ┬╖ O-proj ┬╖ residual ┬╖ LN ┬╖ FFN-up ┬╖ SiLU ┬╖ FFN-down ┬╖ residual). The MOAT: at decode batch=1 the per-op compute is tiny (~5 ┬╡s) vs the per-launch overhead (~1 ┬╡s warm ├Ч 17 launches = 17 ┬╡s in eager), so launch-count reduction transfers almost 1:1 into wall reduction. This is the ┬з5f / ┬з5a axis extended to a full transformer layer's worth of ops тАФ the regime where vLLM / PyTorch eager per-token decode bleeds the most.

**Shape**: GPT-2-small d=768, n_heads=12, head_dim=64, kv_cache_len L=512 (representative mid-context decode step).

- [x] **F-FUSION-AUTOREGRESSIVE-DECODE structural** ЁЯФ╡ SUPPORTED-FORMAL тАФ `$0` deterministic oracle (compiled hexa `oracle.hexa`, exit 0): per layer per token **fused 2 launches vs eager 17 (8.5├Ч fewer)**; **temp-HBM round-trip 0 B vs 112 656 B (100% eliminated)**; closed-form launch-bound wall projection from MEASURED L=1 ┬╡s/launch warm overhead (`F-RFC067-PB-TIMING`) gives **70.6%** wall reduction (eager 17 ┬╡s vs fused max(5 ┬╡s, 2 ┬╡s)=5 ┬╡s); compute-saturated floor **тЙе30%** unconditional (the 9 elementwise/norm/residual eager launches collapse into 0 in fused, ~9 ┬╡s overhead saved no matter what). For a 12-layer model: fused **24 launches/token vs eager 204** (8.5├Ч fewer); fused **0 vs eager ~1.35 MiB temp-HBM/token**.
- [x] **ptxas-clean** тАФ sm_80 + sm_90 RC=0 on both fused (2 mega-kernels: 32+27 regs ┬╖ 40 960+16 384 B smem ┬╖ 0 spill) and eager (17 entries: 8тАУ26 regs each ┬╖ 0 spill). sm_120 reached via `cuModuleLoadDataEx` driver-JIT (forward-compat, same path as `F-FUSION-LAUNCH-AMORT` / `F-FUSION-ATTN-WMMA`). Smem 40 960 B fits the 49 152 B/block sm_80/sm_90 envelope.
- [x] **F-FUSION-AUTOREGRESSIVE-DECODE-WALL (round-9 timed silicon, FIRED 2026-05-26) тАФ ЁЯФ┤ FALSIFIED** тАФ host harness (`tool/r9_walls/ar_host.c`) + f64 CPU reference + per-row-scaled rel тЙд 1e-2 + NaN/Inf hard-fail; cuEvent 20 warmup / 200 timed median on ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120 (0% util pre-fire each L). Sweep L тИИ {64,256,512,1024,2048}. **NUMERIC FAIL both fused (max_relтЙИ1.61) and eager (max_relтЙИ1.9)** тАФ the merged `decode_attn_fused` omits real online-softmax (uses `inv_sqrt_hd` placeholder weight + un-zeroed smem-atomic RMSNorm), and eager `k1_rmsnorm` is placeholder unit-scale + `k9_softmax` has no max-subtract/normalise (both PTX are R8 STRUCTURAL STUBS, not numerically-complete). **WALL: fused FLAT ~80 ms тИАL vs eager ~1.89тЖТ1.98 ms тЖТ fused ~40-42├Ч SLOWER at EVERY L** (pct_above_eager тИТ4138 %@L=64 тЖТ тИТ3957 %@L=2048). **NO launch-bound win, NO crossover** тАФ the projected 70.6 % does NOT materialise. ROOT CAUSE: `decode_attn_fused` is ONE CTA of 768 threads (single SM тЙИ 1/48 GPU, O(d┬▓) per-thread QKV GEMV, serial smem-atomic RMSNorm); the 17 tiny eager kernels @ ~0.11 ms total ~1.9 ms still beat one 80 ms mega-kernel тАФ the binding constraint is intra-kernel single-CTA serialisation, NOT launch count. The R8 structural moat (2 vs 17 launches, 8.5├Ч; 100 % temp-HBM elim) is REAL but does NOT convert. Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-autoregressive-decode/F-FUSION-AUTOREGRESSIVE-DECODE-TIMED.txt`.
- [ ] **F-FUSION-AUTOREGRESSIVE-COMPLETE (round-12 COMPLETE + properly-parallelized, FIRED 2026-05-26) тАФ ЁЯЯа SUB-THRESHOLD launch-bound WIN** тАФ the R9 closing note's prescription delivered: a COMPLETE fused 2-mega-kernel decode (real RMSNorm + Q/K/V GEMV + KV-cache append + masked single-q FLASH attention with online softmax + O-proj + RMSNorm + SwiGLU), **multi-CTA cooperative grid** (`cuLaunchCooperativeKernel` + `grid.sync()`), GEMV rows striped across ALL grid warps (coalesced warp-coop dots), attention KEYS parallelized across KW warps/head + flash-merge тАФ NOT the R9 single-CTA single-thread-per-row stub. Fired on ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120 (0% util pre-fire), cuEvent 20 warmup + 200 median (median-of-3), L тИИ {64..4096}, vs a **FAIR eager 18-launch baseline** (R11 lesson: the first eager `attn_av` was a CTA/head serial-over-L **strawman** = 0.076 ms@L4096 dominating the layer тЖТ rewrote key-parallel = 0.0069 ms, 10├Ч; all sub-kernels now coalesced/parallel). **NUMERIC PASS all L** (fused rel тЙд 3.2e-5, eager rel тЙд 1.6e-5, nan_inf=0). **WALL (median-of-3, fused/eager): L=64 0.936 (+6.4%) ┬╖ L=256 0.966 (+3.4%) ┬╖ L=512 0.892 (+10.8%) ┬╖ L=1024 0.889 (+11.1%, best) ┬╖ L=1536 1.189 (тИТ18.9%, CROSSOVER) ┬╖ L=2048 1.225 (тИТ22.5%) ┬╖ L=4096 1.044 (тИТ4.4%)**. Fusion WINS the launch-bound regime (L тЙд 1024) but NOT тЙе30% at any L. Launch-saving realized тЙИ 8.2 ┬╡s @ L=1024 = ~40% of net-theoretical 20.4 ┬╡s/layer (gross launch (18тИТ2)├Ч1.81 ┬╡s = 28.9 ┬╡s тИТ grid.sync 10├Ч0.85 ┬╡s = 8.5 ┬╡s). WHAT SWAMPED IT: fused body slightly slower than the sum of eager's per-op kernel bodies тАФ serial flash-merge over KW key-partials + 10 `grid.sync` barriers serialize phases (defeats cross-kernel latency hiding) + single global cooperative-grid config can't retune occupancy per phase. **R12 falsifier NOT-falsified-numeric but тЯи30%-gate NOT clearedтЯй тЖТ ЁЯЯа.** Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-autoregressive-complete/F-FUSION-AUTOREGRESSIVE-COMPLETE.txt`; artifact `archive/fires/fusion_autoregressive_complete_2026_05_26/`.
- [ ] **┬з10 axis-E row** тАФ closure lane (NOT a scoreboard slot; closure remains 8/8 тЬЕ). **R9 timed wall ЁЯФ┤ FALSIFIED (single-CTA stub); R12 COMPLETE+parallelized ЁЯЯа SUB-THRESHOLD** тАФ fusion now WINS the launch-bound regime L тЙд 1024 by +3..+11% (corrects R9's 40├Ч regression: the body was the problem, not the launch logic) but the realized launch-saving is below the 30% gate, and crossover to loss at L ~ 1536 once attention goes compute/memory-bound. **Axis-E stays `[ ]`** тАФ the launch-bound fusion moat is REAL for decode but sub-threshold. Next: collapse RMSNorm grid.sync (pre-pass), warp-reduce flash-merge, per-phase occupancy via sm_90 cluster-launch тАФ or accept decode as a sub-threshold launch-bound win and pursue multi-layer whole-model fusion where the per-layer saving compounds ├ЧN_layers.

Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-autoregressive-decode/F-FUSION-AUTOREGRESSIVE-DECODE.txt`; discovery `.discoveries/fusion-autoregressive-decode.tape`; CLAIMS.tape `@C fusion_autoregressive_decode_structural`; artifact `archive/fires/fusion_autoregressive_decode_2026_05_25/` (fused_decode.ptx + eager_decode.ptx + oracle.hexa + oracle_output.txt + ptxas_clean.log + FIRE.md). No LLVM (@F f1). No C-transpile change (@F f2). CPU codegen untouched (hand-emit PTX, pure ASCII).

**Verdict framing**: "structural launches per token per layer: hexa **2** vs eager **17** тАФ vLLM / PyTorch API per-call structure forbids the fusion; projected launch-bound wall тЙе**70%** above eager per-token (round-9 timed will confirm)."
