## 2 ┬╖ Next layer (concrete, scope-bounded тАФ pick one to start)

### 2a тАФ Source-to-silicon e2e closure (RFC 068 last gap)

Today's silicon fires used hand-emit PTX (codegen verification via `nvptx_lower_test` smoke; silicon via fire). The remaining gap: a `.hexa` source file with `@gpu_kernel fn f16_vadd(...)` lowering through HIR тЖТ MIR тЖТ codegen_emit_ptx_sm80 тЖТ ptxas тЖТ fire.

- [ ] **source kernel fixture** тАФ write `test/rfc068_f16_vadd_e2e.hexa` with `@gpu_kernel fn f16_vadd(a: [f16], b: [f16], c: [f16], n: i64)` body
- [ ] **HIR тЖТ MIR lowering** тАФ verify `let t: f16 = a[i] + b[i]` lowers to `STMT_LOAD .f16 + STMT_BINOP add_f16 + STMT_STORE .f16` with precision tag propagated
- [ ] **MFunc.gpu_kind = KERNEL** тАФ `@gpu_kernel` annotation parse + lowering hooked
- [ ] **codegen emits launchable PTX** тАФ `.visible .entry` + `.param .u64` quartet (a/b/c/n) + body
- [ ] **ptxas-clean check** тАФ emitted PTX passes `ptxas -arch=sm_80`
- [ ] **fire on ubu-2** тАФ driver-JIT + cuLaunchKernel + compare to f64 reference
- [ ] **`F-RFC068-E2E-NUMERIC-EQ`** PASS тАФ full source-to-silicon chain byte-eq closure
- [ ] **commit** тАФ same `archive/fires/` pattern as PR #189

### 2a finding (2026-05-20): build pipeline gap analysis

The blocker is NOT in `self/main.hexa::cmd_build` `--target=` validation
(adding a `nvptx64-*` branch there is one-line edit). The substantive
gap is the BUILD PIPELINE itself:

```
Current `hexa build` (CPU targets):
  src.hexa тЖТ module_loader (flatten) тЖТ hexa_v2 transpiler (.c)
           тЖТ clang/zig cc тЖТ native binary

Required for NVPTX:
  src.hexa тЖТ module_loader (flatten) тЖТ in-hexa compiler self-host
           тЖТ MIR тЖТ codegen_emit_ptx_sm80 тЖТ PTX text
```

`hexa_v2` is the **bootstrap transpiler** that emits C тАФ it doesn't
know about NVPTX. The NVPTX codegen lives in `compiler/codegen/
nvptx_target.hexa` and is invoked only from within the in-hexa
self-host pipeline (which today produces CPU artifacts via the
existing `compiler/*` tree, not via `hexa_v2`).

To wire `hexa build --target=nvptx64-*` properly, options are:
- (A) **Internal emit-driver pattern** тАФ `cmd_build` synthesizes a
  small driver `import src.hexa + compiler/codegen/nvptx_target.hexa`
  and prints `codegen_emit_ptx_sm80(...)`. Substantial: requires
  exposing the full compiler pipeline as a callable.
- (B) **Compiler self-host on NVPTX** тАФ the in-hexa compiler IS
  the build path for `--target=nvptx64`. Aligned with north-star тСб
  (self-host already PROVEN for CPU at fixpoint per memory
  `project_compiler_native_self_host_fixpoint`); extending to
  NVPTX is the natural next step.
- (C) **Out-of-band emit driver** тАФ keep using the external script
  pattern from PR #82 (`tool/dispatch_*.sh`). Today's 8 fires
  successfully demonstrate this works. **No `hexa build` wiring
  required** for the actual silicon-validation path.

Choice for this session: **(C)** тАФ defer (A)/(B) as multi-session
campaigns. The ┬з1 ledger shows all silicon-fires landed via the
out-of-band pattern; full source-to-silicon `hexa build --target=
nvptx64-*` is a strategic infrastructure cycle for a separate
session.

**Update 2026-05-20 (RFC 071 P0 scaffold landed):** This gap is now
formally tracked as RFC 071 тАФ see
`docs/rfc/rfc_drafts_2026_05_20/rfc_071_source_to_silicon_e2e.md`. P0
landed the `cmd_build` target-string recognition for
`nvptx64-nvidia-cuda-sm80` / `sm90` / `sm120` (informative deferred
exit + RFC pointer; CPU codegen path byte-identical, no LLVM, no new
C-transpile architecture per `@F f1`/`@F f2`). P1-P4 (real dispatch +
emit-driver module + module_loader bridge + e2e silicon fire) are
explicitly deferred multi-cycle work governed by the F-RFC071-* falsifier
battery. Approach **A (internal emit-driver synthesis)** is the
recommended P1-P2 path; **B (compiler self-host on NVPTX)** is the
P3+ convergence path once north-star тСб's CPU self-host campaign
default-flips. Approach C remains the codegen-author fast iteration
shell тАФ RFC 071 introduces a new path, not a replacement.

**Update 2026-05-20 (RFC 071 P1+P2 landed):** P1 replaced the
deferred-print + exit(1) branch with a call to
`self/main.hexa::_build_nvptx_emit_driver(src, sm_arch)` (F-RFC071-
TARGET-ACCEPT PASS). P2 added the spec sibling module
`compiler/cli/build_nvptx.hexa` defining
`pub fn build_nvptx_emit_driver(src_path, sm_arch) -> int` with a
canned stub PTX writer (`.version 7.0` / `.target sm_NN` /
`.address_size 64` / `.visible .entry _hexa_smoke() { ret; }`) тАФ
F-RFC071-EMIT-DRIVER-INVOKE PASS as a STUB. **Honest punt (@D g3):**
the body emits CANNED PTX тАФ F-RFC071-MODULE-LOADER-BRIDGE is
INTENTIONALLY deferred until P2.1 wires `codegen_emit_ptx_sm80(mir)`
(parse тЖТ check тЖТ lower тЖТ codegen chain documented in the module
docstring). CPU codegen byte-identical (`F-RFC055-CPU-CODEGEN-
UNTOUCHED` PASS by md5; @F f1/@F f2 honored). ┬з10 box `[ ] ┬з12 P4+
source-to-silicon e2e` stays `[ ]` per @D g3 тАФ only the P4 numeric-eq
falsifier flips it.

### 2b тАФ Multi-tile WMMA GEMM K-loop (RFC 067 ┬з3 P4 spec form)

PR #191 closed the *single-tile* WMMA fire. The RFC 067 ┬з3 P4 spec asks for 64├Ч64 GEMM = 4├Ч4 output tiles ├Ч 4 K-tiles = 64 `wmma.mma` calls with `.shared` staging.

- [ ] **multi-tile kernel** тАФ hand-emit `wmma_64x64.ptx` with explicit 4├Ч4├Ч4 nested loops
- [ ] **`.shared` staging slot allocation** тАФ 4 KB shared mem for A/B double-buffer tiles
- [ ] **K-loop accumulator carry** тАФ C fragment reuse across K-tile iterations (no spill)
- [ ] **host launcher** тАФ `tool/r067_p4_multi_host.c` mirrors `r067_p4_host.c` but 64├Ч64
- [ ] **fire on ubu-2 + compare to FP32 reference** тАФ `тЙд 1e-2 rel error` tolerance (the canonical f16-mul-f32-acc bound)
- [ ] **`F-RFC067-TILE-LOOP-NUMERIC-MULTI`** PASS
- [ ] **codegen-side hexa equivalent** тАФ synthesize MFunc with multi-block K-loop body + multi-`gpu_wmma_mma` STMT_CALL emit

### 2c тАФ Codegen-side BF16 silicon reconcile

Today's PR #193 reconciled `f16 тЖТ b16` storage; bf16 reg type still trips ptxas 12.0 `.reg .bf16` parse.

- [ ] **PTX 7.8 toolchain bump probe** тАФ test bf16 acceptance on `.version 8.0` / `.version 8.x` PTX targets
- [ ] **`add.bf16` instruction support** тАФ verify ptxas accepts the bf16 arithmetic path
- [ ] **hexa codegen flip** тАФ if PTX 8.x parses cleanly, emit `.version 8.0` + native `.reg .bf16` decl; else stay with `.reg .b16` and use bitcast
- [ ] **bf16 vec-add fire** тАФ same pattern as PR #189 but bf16 inputs
- [ ] **`F-RFC068-NUMERIC-EQ-BF16`** PASS

### 2d тАФ Hexa-native dispatch (replace direct-bash + sidesetep HEXA_FIRST_WARN)

PR #189/#190/#191 fires used direct one-shot bash; sustained automation needs hexa-native.

- [x] **stdlib/cloud dispatch primer** тАФ `tool/dispatch_gpu_fire.hexa` orchestrates the whole fire (upload тЖТ nvcc тЖТ fire тЖТ pull) through `stdlib/cloud` `cloud_copy_to_opts` / `cloud_exec_opts` / `cloud_copy_from_opts`. All shell-out rides `exec_capture` (codegen-wired) inside the cloud module тАФ NOT `exec_argv` (no codegen branch тЖТ would fail to link). f1/f2 preserved (no codegen touched).
- [x] **`tool/dispatch_gpu_fire.hexa`** тАФ generic hexa-native fire dispatcher. Args `<host.c> <ptx>[,<ptx>...] [target-host]` + `--out/--remote/--result/--port/--insecure/--kernel`. Multi-PTX (comma-sep, argv-order). **Parses rc=0** (`hexa parse`) AND **compiles+links clean** (`hexa build` тЖТ runnable arm64 binary, only harmless `runtime.h` comment warnings).
- [x] **smoke verify** тАФ re-fired the RFC 055-P2 vec-add + naive-GEMM PTX (the kernels backing `dispatch_r055_p2_gemm.sh`) via the new dispatcher on ubu-2 RTX 5070. **result.json byte-identical to the recorded `state/rfc055_p2_2026_05_20/result.json`** (md5 `cd249eeb7879031e8fee53994d01e475` both sides) тАФ all 4 falsifiers PASS, vec-add max|╬Ф|=0 mismatches=0/1024, GEMM max|╬Ф|=0 mismatches=0/4096. fire.log falsifier lines identical. $0.
- [x] **migrate** тАФ `tool/dispatch_r055_p2_gemm.sh` removed (`git rm`); the hexa dispatcher re-fires the same kernels at measured byte-eq. Invoke: `dispatch_gpu_fire tool/r055_p2_host.c <vec_add.ptx>,<gemm.ptx> ubu-2`.

### 2e тАФ `cp.async` pipelining (sm_80+) тАФ performance, not correctness

- [ ] **PTX opcode constants** тАФ `PTX_OP_CP_ASYNC_F16`, `PTX_OP_CP_ASYNC_COMMIT_GROUP`, `PTX_OP_CP_ASYNC_WAIT_GROUP`
- [ ] **codegen seam** тАФ when WMMA kernel's K-loop body references `.shared` storage, emit `cp.async.cg.shared.global` for prefetch
- [ ] **double-buffer pattern** тАФ two `.shared` staging slots; alternating fill/use
- [ ] **fire vs no-`cp.async` baseline** тАФ same numeric output, measure throughput gain
- [ ] **`F-RFC067-CP-ASYNC-PERF`** тАФ throughput delta documented (тЙе 1.3├Ч target)

---

## 3 ┬╖ Mid-term (deferred, scoped but multi-cycle)

### 3a тАФ Additional dtypes

- [ ] **bf16 full silicon validation** (depends on 2c)
- [ ] **tf32 support** тАФ `mma.sync.aligned.row.col.m16n16k8.f32.tf32.tf32.f32` for fp32 acceleration
- [ ] **int8 / int4** тАФ quantization-friendly types; `dp4a` / `dp2a` instructions
- [x] **fp8 e4m3 / e5m2** (Hopper sm_90+) тАФ codegen scaffold landed (RFC 068 ┬з3): `NVPTX_RKIND_F8_E4M3` / `_F8_E5M2` constants + `%fe3<id>` / `%fe5<id>` reg banks (silicon-canonical `.b8` container per PTX ISA ┬з5.4.1 + ┬з9.7.13.5) + classifier short-circuit on `.f8_e4m3` / `.f8_e5m2` precision tag + `ld.global.b8` / `st.global.b8` ld/st dispatch + Case 26/27 lower_test (ld/st round-trip, bank-isolation negative guard). **No silicon fire** тАФ fp8 WMMA mnemonic family (`wmma.mma.sync...e4m3.e4m3.f32`) + sub-byte ABI (kernel-arg packing, addr alignment) + parser-side `@f8_*` named-type grammar are follow-on cycles.
- [ ] **posit** тАФ custom dtype emission (lattice-friendly arithmetic; experimental)
- [ ] **MXFP4 / NVFP4** тАФ Blackwell sm_120+ dtypes if applicable to RTX 5070

### 3b тАФ Tensor Core families beyond canonical

- [ ] **bf16├Чbf16тЖТf32** family тАФ flip `_nvptx_wmma_mnemonic_family` selector
- [ ] **f16├Чf16тЖТf16** family тАФ accumulation in `.f16` (lower precision)
- [ ] **tf32├Чtf32тЖТf32** (Ampere+) тАФ TF32 default precision GEMM
- [ ] **fp8 wgmma** (Hopper sm_90+) тАФ `wgmma.mma_async` (asynchronous warp-group)
- [ ] **wgmma 64x64x16, 64x128x16** large tiles тАФ larger working tile geometry
- [ ] **m8n8k16 / m16n8k8** non-standard shapes тАФ flexible mnemonic table

### 3c тАФ Memory hierarchy + addressing

- [ ] **`.shared` register-tiling helpers** тАФ auto-staging on `gpu_*` op patterns
- [ ] **`.local` scratch space** тАФ register-spill destination for large kernels
- [ ] **`.const` constant bank** тАФ for kernel-invariant LUTs
- [ ] **`ld.cs` / `ld.lu` cache hints** тАФ streaming / last-use semantics
- [ ] **TMA (Tensor Memory Accelerator) sm_90+** тАФ `cp.async.bulk.tensor.<dim>d.shared.global`
- [ ] **Async barriers** тАФ `mbarrier.init`, `mbarrier.arrive`, `mbarrier.wait`

### 3d тАФ Optimization passes

- [ ] **Unroll factor>4 with register-pressure analysis** тАФ refuse factor=N if predicted register count > 64
- [ ] **Loop-carried dependency analysis** тАФ true LCD detection (currently trusts user)
- [ ] **Loop fusion** тАФ adjacent kernels with shared address тЖТ single launch
- [ ] **Software pipelining** тАФ interleave K-loop iterations
- [ ] **Constant folding through PTX** тАФ known-constant operands тЖТ immediate
- [ ] **Dead-code elimination** тАФ operations whose results are never read
- [ ] **Register allocation** тАФ proper graph coloring (currently 1:1 LocalтЖТreg)
- [ ] **Polyhedral / affine loop transformation** тАФ far-future advanced opt

### 3e тАФ Source-level features (`@gpu_kernel` ergonomics)

- [ ] **`@gpu_kernel` attribute parse** тАФ currently honored at lowering; verify parser surface
- [ ] **`@shared` annotation** тАФ declare a `let` as shared-memory-resident
- [ ] **`@warp_intrinsic` annotation** тАФ opt-in warp-shuffle intrinsics
- [ ] **`gpu_launch` builtin** тАФ host-side `gpu_launch<<<grid, block>>>(kernel, args...)` lowering
- [ ] **`gpu_launch_async` / `gpu_event`** тАФ CUDA stream + event API equivalents
- [ ] **`gpu_sync()` host-side** тАФ `cudaDeviceSynchronize` wrapper
- [ ] **Source-level `gpu_atomic_*` family** тАФ atomic ops covering add/cas/exch/min/max
- [ ] **Source-level `gpu_block_*` reductions** тАФ sum / max / argmax via `bar.sync` + shared

### 3f тАФ Multi-vendor (downstream тАФ orthogonal to NVPTX)

- [ ] **HIP/AMD ROCm backend** тАФ `gfx*` target dispatch (RFC 075 P0 scaffold landed: `compiler/codegen/rocm_target.hexa` + `rocm_lower_test.hexa` тАФ emit stub returns `""`, P1+ multi-session BLOCKED тАФ no AMD GPU in pool, cycle cannot silicon-fire-validate)
- [x] **Metal Performance Shaders** ЁЯЫ╕ тАФ Apple Silicon GPU (`@gpu_kernel` тЖТ MSL source text; RFC 075 P1+P2+P3 codegen-only LANDED 2026-05-20 Campaign C: `compiler/codegen/metal_target.hexa` emits full MSL vec-add kernel source `kernel void vec_add(device const float* a [[buffer(0)]], ..., uint i [[thread_position_in_grid]]) { c[i] = a[i] + b[i]; }` for vec-add-shaped MIR; F-RFC075-METAL-EMIT-VEC-ADD PASS via 15-substring smoke `metal_lower_test.hexa`; **P4 silicon-fire LANDED 2026-05-21** тАФ `xcrun -sdk macosx metal` + `metallib` + Swift `MTLComputePipelineState` dispatch on Apple M3 GPU. N=1024 FP32 vec-add max|╬Ф|=0.0 byte_mismatch=0/1024. F-RFC075-METAL-NUMERIC-EQ PASS. Artifact: `archive/fires/rfc075_metal_p4_2026_05_21/`)
- [ ] **Intel oneAPI / Level Zero / SPIR-V** тАФ Intel iGPU / Xe substrate (deferred to follow-on RFC, see RFC 075 ┬з2)
- [ ] **WebGPU / SPIR-V** тАФ browser substrate
- [ ] **Cross-vendor abstraction layer** тАФ shared IR pre-target

---

## 4 ┬╖ Performance benchmarking + competitive positioning

### 4a тАФ Throughput baselines (vs vendor)

- [ ] **HGEMM throughput** тАФ hexa-emit vs cuBLAS HGEMM on identical (M,N,K)
- [ ] **SGEMM throughput** тАФ hexa-emit vs cuBLAS SGEMM
- [ ] **FP64 GEMM** тАФ hexa-emit vs cuBLAS DGEMM
- [ ] **vec-add bandwidth** тАФ hexa-emit vs CUDA stream `cudaMemcpy` (memory-bound)
- [ ] **kernel-launch overhead** тАФ hexa-emit vs CUDA driver native (microseconds)

### 4b тАФ End-to-end workload (flame integration)

- [x] **flame d=768┬╖12L transformer 1 step wall** тАФ hexa-emit (forge) **20-43% faster** vs PyTorch eager (memory: `project_flame_phase4d9_closure`, commit `28e9d648`)
- [ ] **flame d=4096 LLaMA-3 8B inference latency** тАФ single-token autoregressive
- [ ] **flame mixture-of-experts dispatch** тАФ sparse expert routing on GPU
- [ ] **flame flash-attention 2 fused kernel** тАФ vs `xformers.ops.memory_efficient_attention`

### 4c тАФ vs alternative GPU compiler stacks

- [ ] **vs Triton** тАФ same kernels in hexa vs Triton DSL
- [ ] **vs Mojo** тАФ heavy GPU kernels in hexa vs Mojo MAX
- [ ] **vs Halide-GPU** тАФ algorithm + schedule split comparison
- [ ] **vs ThunderKittens** тАФ single-file abstraction over wmma
- [ ] **vs CUTLASS** тАФ template-based GEMM library

### 4d тАФ vs cuBLAS-using stacks (where hexa structural advantage applies)

- [ ] **PyTorch eager (uses cuBLAS+cuDNN+ATen)** тАФ already partially measured (flame 4-D-9 closure)
- [ ] **JAX (XLA-based; uses cuBLAS via XLA)** тАФ comparable architecture, more aggressive fusion
- [ ] **TensorFlow eager** тАФ older but still widely deployed
- [ ] **MLX (Apple ML)** тАФ Metal-based stack on M-series
- [ ] **TinyGrad** тАФ minimalist Python-based codegen

---

## 5 ┬╖ Niches where hexa structurally beats cuBLAS (potential moat)

### 5a тАФ Fusion that cuBLAS can't do

- [ ] **GEMM + epilogue fusion** тАФ GEMM + bias_add + ReLU + dropout in single kernel (cuBLAS-LT does some, but limited). **STRUCTURAL FINDING 2026-05-25** (`F-FUSION-EPILOGUE-GEMM-BIAS-GELU`): fused `GeLU(A@B + bias)` hexa-emit kernel proven (by `$0` deterministic oracle, compiled hexa) to use **1 launch + 1├Ч M├ЧN HBM C-write** vs cuBLAS-using stack **3 + 3├Ч** = **66.667 % reduction in BOTH launch-count AND HBM-write-traffic** at LLaMA-7B FFN shape (M=4096 N=11008 K=4096); PTX ptxas-clean sm_80 (RC=0, 0 spill). ЁЯФ╡ structural-formal. Timed wall DEFERRED to serial follow-up. Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_epilogue_gemm_bias_gelu_2026_05_25/`
- [ ] **Attention scoring fusion** тАФ Q@K^T + softmax + V@ in single kernel (flash-attn pattern)
- [ ] **MoE dispatch + GEMM + reduce** тАФ single kernel from gate to output
- [ ] **LayerNorm + GEMM fusion** тАФ pre-layer-norm fused with GEMM weights
- [ ] **AdamW step fusion** тАФ optimizer + parameter update fused with gradient compute

### 5b тАФ Compile-time specialization

- [ ] **Static shape specialization** тАФ known-(M,N,K) kernels avoid all runtime branches
- [ ] **Dead-output elimination** тАФ masked outputs / pruned channels removed at compile time
- [ ] **Sparsity-pattern specialization** тАФ block-sparse / structured-sparse layouts as compile-time facts
- [ ] **Mixed-precision auto-selection** тАФ picker chooses dtype per layer based on compile-time error analysis

### 5c тАФ Custom dtypes / non-IEEE arithmetic

- [ ] **n=6 lattice primitives** тАФ RFC 057 / hexa-arch chip тАФ non-binary lattice math on GPU
- [ ] **Posit arithmetic** тАФ variable-precision posit emit
- [ ] **Interval arithmetic** тАФ error-bounded compute
- [ ] **Stochastic rounding** тАФ quantization-friendly random rounding

### 5d тАФ Whole-program autograd-aware

- [x] **flame `ag_tape` / `ag_derive`** тАФ already SD1-SD6 landed (PRs in main history)
- [ ] **GPU kernel fusion across autograd boundaries** тАФ forward + backward kernels fused
- [ ] **Compile-time gradient symbolic simplification** тАФ vs PyTorch's autograd runtime tape

### 5e тАФ Non-NVIDIA hardware

- [ ] **Apple M-series Metal Performance Shaders** тАФ Apple-silicon GPUs (currently flame uses CPU on M-series)
- [ ] **AMD MI300 / MI350** тАФ ROCm HIP backend
- [ ] **Intel Xe / Arc** тАФ oneAPI / Level Zero
- [ ] **Multi-vendor unified kernel** тАФ same `@gpu_kernel` lowered to multiple backends

### 5f тАФ Launch-overhead amortization (PyTorch eager / library-call stacks lose here)

- [x] **flame d=768┬╖12L transformer тАФ 20-43% faster than PyTorch eager** тАФ already measured (`project_flame_phase4d9_closure`). PyTorch eager pays per-op kernel launch overhead; cuBLAS calls cost тЙе5 ╬╝s each. Hexa whole-program fusion eliminates the per-op launch path
- [x] **F-FUSION-LAUNCH-AMORT тАФ fused 5-op chain $0 oracle + ptxas-clean (2026-05-25, ┬з1h)** ЁЯЫ╕ тАФ isolated launch-amortization case: fused `y = residual + scale┬╖GeLU(a┬╖x+b)` (mul┬╖add┬╖gelu┬╖mul-scale┬╖add-resid) in **1 launch / 3 HBM transfers per elem** vs per-op baseline **5 launches / 11 transfers**. Deterministic oracle (exit 0) + closed-form projection from measured L=1 ┬╡s (┬з1g): launch-bound 80%, bandwidth-bound 72.7%, **тЙе30% UNCONDITIONAL across all n** (30%-crossover n\* negative). ptxas-clean sm_80 both modules (0 spill). Timed silicon wall DEFERRED-to-serial. Artifact: `archive/fires/gpu_fusion_launch_amort_2026_05_25/`
- [ ] **No PyBind11 / no ATen dispatch overhead** тАФ cuBLAS via PyTorch goes through Python тЖТ C++ Tensor тЖТ ATen тЖТ CUDA stream тЖТ cuBLAS handle. Hexa-emit directly compiled into the binary
- [ ] **Static kernel selection** тАФ cuBLAS-LT runtime heuristic picks an algorithm; hexa compile-time selects + bakes the algorithm
- [ ] **Single-shot binary** тАФ no shared library boundary, no `cudaGetSymbolAddress`, no driver-level dispatch table

### 5g тАФ Operator-specific surgical override

- [ ] **Replace one kernel mid-pipeline** тАФ cuBLAS is monolithic API; hexa codegen lets a single GEMM in a chain be hand-tuned while the rest of the pipeline stays unchanged
- [ ] **Per-call-site precision** тАФ same logical GEMM compiled with different precision per call site (cuBLAS forces uniform-handle precision)
- [ ] **Mixed-precision in single kernel** тАФ f16 A ├Ч f16 B тЖТ f32 accum тЖТ bf16 store, all in one kernel; cuBLAS API forces handle-uniform dtype
- [ ] **Custom layout / striding** тАФ cuBLAS has limited stride options; hexa per-kernel custom layouts (e.g., interleaved tile arrangements)

### 5h тАФ Compile-time error / safety analysis

- [ ] **Static overflow check** тАФ known input ranges + arithmetic chain тЖТ compile-time overflow risk warning (cuBLAS = runtime only, often silent)
- [ ] **Compile-time NaN-Inf propagation reasoning** тАФ track which operations could introduce NaN/Inf based on input domain analysis
- [ ] **Numerical-stability lint** тАФ flag patterns like `large - small` that lose precision; cuBLAS users have no static signal
- [ ] **Determinism-mode at compile-time** тАФ `@deterministic` annotation switches to deterministic-reduction emit at codegen; cuBLAS's `CUBLAS_PEDANTIC_MATH` is a runtime flag that costs perf

### 5i тАФ Source-level visibility + ergonomics

- [ ] **`.so` blob vs source emit** тАФ cuBLAS is closed-source binary; hexa users see + modify the emit path. Bug-fix loop: cuBLAS = file ticket + wait; hexa = patch source + rebuild
- [ ] **`hexa gpu disasm`** тАФ view exact SASS via `cuobjdump`; cuBLAS too but harder to correlate to user code (the high-level mapping is lost in the closed binary)
- [ ] **Single-language stack** тАФ host + device + autograd all in hexa-lang; cuBLAS-using stacks need Python/C++/CUDA polyglot
- [ ] **No vendor-lock-in path** тАФ hexa codegen targets backend-agnostic IR; cuBLAS hard-binds to NVIDIA

### 5j тАФ Algorithmic flexibility (cuBLAS = limited operator surface)

- [ ] **FlashAttention-style fused softmax + attention** тАФ already a paper-derived pattern; cuBLAS doesn't cover the attention-block pattern directly (xformers / FlashAttention ы│ДыПД library)
- [ ] **Online softmax** тАФ single-pass numerically stable softmax (cuBLAS = no softmax at all)
- [ ] **Block-sparse / structured-sparse GEMM** тАФ cuBLAS = dense only (sparse is cuSPARSE ы│ДыПД)
- [ ] **Custom reductions** тАФ cuBLAS has SUM/MAX; arbitrary reduction (LogSumExp / soft-argmax) hand-written
- [ ] **Top-k / argmax fused with GEMM** тАФ cuBLAS = GEMM only; hexa can fuse arbitrary epilogue

### 5k тАФ Domain-specific kernel libraries (whole-program co-design)

- [x] **flame `ag_*` autograd-aware GEMM family** тАФ SD1-SD10 vjp registry landed; GEMM kernels know about gradients (memory: `project_flame_mk2_cycle_2026_05_19`)
- [ ] **sim_universe lattice GEMM** тАФ non-binary lattice arithmetic on GPU (RFC 057 bridge)
- [ ] **quantum amplitude-update kernels** тАФ `stdlib/quantum` state-vector simulation (cuBLAS = no amplitude ops)
- [ ] **flame layer-fused training kernel** тАФ forward + backward + AdamW + grad-clip in single kernel emit
- [ ] **NN-specific HEXA primitives** тАФ `softmax`, `layer_norm`, `RoPE`, `swiglu` as first-class compiler-aware ops

### 5l тАФ Edge / embedded / standalone deployment

- [ ] **Standalone cubin embed** тАФ `hexa build` produces a binary with embedded `.cubin`; no separate cuBLAS .so dependency
- [ ] **AOT compilation** тАФ kernel compiled once at build time; no runtime cuBLAS JIT
- [ ] **Multi-arch fat binary** тАФ embed PTX for sm_70 + sm_80 + sm_90 in one cubin via hexa codegen
- [ ] **NVIDIA-runtime-free deployment** тАФ minimal driver-only deployment surface (no cuBLAS/cuDNN required)
- [ ] **Containerized cubin** тАФ single-binary container without `libcublas.so.12` dependency

### 5m тАФ Measured wins to-date (g3-honest claims)

- [x] **flame d=768┬╖12L 1-step wall**: hexa-emit 191-268s vs PyTorch-eager 336.85s = **20-43% faster** (commit `28e9d648`, memory `project_flame_phase4d9_closure`)
- [x] **cp.async pipelining ~7% slower than no-async at K=64**: honest negative perf measurement (PR #207) тАФ proves the codegen path works + sets the boundary where cp.async overhead amortizes (large K)
- [x] **WMMA + multi-warp grid + multi-K-tile + cp.async + tf32**: 5 distinct WMMA-family kernel patterns all silicon-validated max\|╬Ф\|=0 vs FP32 reference (PRs #191/#205/#206/#207/#213)
- [x] **HGEMM throughput vs cuBLAS at M=N=K=256**: hexa-emit **4.0960 TFLOPS** vs cuBLAS GemmEx **8.1907 TFLOPS** = **ratio 0.500 ┬▒0.0002** (6-run variance, sub-0.1% std). Closure criterion "тЙе 50% of cuBLAS HGEMM" **MET at this shape** (PR #214). Caveat (g3): single shape; at larger M/N/K cuBLAS's k-loop unroll + ILP + shared-memory pipelining advantages compound; this single data point does NOT generalize. Multi-tile cp.async (PR #207) not yet integrated into this perf kernel тАФ natural next-cycle.
- [ ] **HGEMM at M=N=KтЙе1024**: pending тАФ scale-up + cp.async integration to test if 0.50├Ч ratio holds or degrades at large shapes (where cuBLAS optimizations matter)
- [x] **PyTorch eager d=1024 12L FP32 PROXY baseline on RTX 5070**: median 1-step wall = **116.286 ms** (std 0.104 ms = 0.089 % of median; peak 5,060 MiB) at d=1024 n_layer=12 batch=2 seq=512 FP32 Adam eager. RFC 072 P1 (this PR). Caveat (g3): this is the L4 ladder rung тАФ RFC 072 ┬з2 spec (d=2048+ 12L) **does not fit** the 12 GB consumer-GPU envelope on PyTorch eager (50,257-token embed+head alone occupies ~5 GiB Adam-state overhead); d=4096 24L full-spec baseline requires H100 80GB multi-session. F-RFC072-WALL-PT-PROXY MEASURED ┬╖ F-RFC072-WALL-PT-FULL DEFERRED.
- [ ] **Whole-program-fusion тЙе 30% over cuBLAS-using stack on a representative LLM workload** тАФ sustained across model variants (flame d=768 partially measured)

---

## 6 ┬╖ Verification + safety

### 6a тАФ Numerical

- [ ] **Bit-exact reference** тАФ every emitted kernel compared to a bit-exact reference (cpu)
- [ ] **ULP-bounded checker** тАФ tolerance-aware compare via a small test harness
- [ ] **Determinism mode** тАФ force deterministic reductions (no atomics, ordered K-loop)
- [ ] **Kahan summation in GEMM K-loop** тАФ error-bounded accumulator
- [ ] **NaN / Inf propagation** тАФ verified across f16 / bf16 underflow / overflow

### 6b тАФ Formal / semantic

- [ ] **PTX emit semantic equivalence proof** тАФ Coq/Lean proof that codegen preserves MIR semantics
- [ ] **Register allocation correctness** тАФ formal proof that allocation never aliases live ranges
- [ ] **Loop-unroll preservation** тАФ proof that unrolled CFG тЙб original CFG semantically

### 6c тАФ Runtime safety

- [ ] **Bounds-check elision** тАФ verified safe when guarded
- [ ] **Race-detection** тАФ static analyzer over shared-memory accesses
- [ ] **Memory-ordering** тАФ `bar.sync` / `mbarrier` placement audit

---

### 7a тАФ Profiling / introspection

- [ ] **PTX register-count reporter** тАФ `ptxas -v` integration into `hexa build`
- [ ] **Occupancy estimator** тАФ given kernel + GPU SM, predict theoretical occupancy
- [ ] **Nsight Compute integration** тАФ emit metadata for profiler attach
- [ ] **CUDA Graph API** тАФ `cuGraphLaunch` for multi-kernel graphs
- [ ] **Driver API vs Runtime API** тАФ pick based on use-case

### 7b тАФ Documentation + examples

- [x] **gpu/SPEC.md** тАФ existing spec doc (per AGENTS.tape mentions)
- [x] **docs/rfc/rfc_drafts_2026_05_20/rfc_06[7-9]_*.md** тАФ 3 RFC drafts
- [ ] **GPU.md** (this file) тАФ domain SSOT roadmap
- [ ] **Tutorial тАФ "first GPU kernel in hexa"** тАФ beginner's onramp
- [ ] **Cookbook тАФ "GEMM patterns from naive to wmma"** тАФ performance evolution

### 7c тАФ Toolchain ergonomics

- [ ] **`hexa gpu build`** тАФ single-command path: source `.hexa` тЖТ PTX тЖТ cubin
- [x] **`hexa gpu fire <kernel> <host>`** тАФ single-command remote fire  (PR #215, 2026-05-20)

- [x] **`hexa gpu lint <ptx>`** тАФ static check on a PTX file (non-ASCII / `.target sm_NN` / `.reg` count / opcode-vs-sm consistency)  (this PR, 2026-05-20)
- [x] **`hexa gpu disasm <ptx>`** тАФ PTX opcode-family histogram via pure-hexa scan (no ptxas/cuobjdump dependency)  (this PR, 2026-05-20)

## 8 ┬╖ Far-future / research questions

### 8a тАФ Beyond NVPTX

- [ ] **PTX тЖТ SASS direct emit** тАФ bypass ptxas, hand-emit GPU machine code
- [ ] **SPIR-V emit** тАФ open-standard GPU IR
- [ ] **MLIR integration** тАФ bridge to upstream MLIR (controversial тАФ vs hexa-native principle)
- [ ] **Cooperative groups API** тАФ multi-block synchronization

### 8b тАФ Auto-tuning

- [ ] **Search-based tile-size selection** тАФ autotune over block/grid/unroll
- [ ] **ML-based scheduling** тАФ neural-net cost model for codegen choices
- [ ] **Random restart for kernel synthesis** тАФ try N variants, pick best

### 8c тАФ Specialized hardware

- [ ] **NVIDIA Grace-Hopper** тАФ CPU+GPU unified memory (`MemcpyDtoH` becomes a no-op)
- [ ] **NVLink / NVSwitch** тАФ multi-GPU collective primitives
- [ ] **AMD Instinct MI300A** тАФ APU-style hexa kernel
- [ ] **Intel Ponte Vecchio** тАФ Xe Matrix Extensions

### 8d тАФ Esoteric / experimental

- [ ] **Quantum GPU bridge** тАФ `stdlib/quantum` + GPU acceleration for state-vector simulation
- [ ] **Lattice n=6 GPU emit** тАФ RFC 057 hexa-arch substrate, but on GPU
- [ ] **Neuromorphic compatibility** тАФ `stdlib/sim_universe` substrate on GPU
- [ ] **Reversible computing primitives** тАФ `gpu_uncompute` for memory-efficient autograd

## 9 ┬╖ Cross-axis dependencies

```
                          [GPU.md root]
                              тФВ
        тФМтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФ╝тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФР
        тФВ                     тФВ                     тФВ
    [┬з12 P4+ chain]       [flame stack]      [forge GPU substrate]
   (codegenтЖТsilicon)    (NN training, north-    (raw cuBLAS/CUDA layer
        тФВ              star тСа measured-PASS)      below flame)
        тФВ                     тФВ                     тФВ
        тФФтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФмтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФ┤тФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФАтФШ
                  тФВ
              [hexa-arch chip]
              (lattice primitives,
              future n=6 ASIC; GPU is
              an interim substrate)
```

- North-star тСа (NN stack) consumes the GPU substrate built here.
- North-star тСб (self-host) is orthogonal (CPU-side; not blocked by GPU).
- North-star тСв (n=6 lattice) тАФ GPU is the INTERIM execution path; final substrate is custom silicon (hexa-arch).

---

## 10 ┬╖ Closure criteria (when is GPU substrate "done"?)

The GPU substrate has finite scope. Closure тЙа "all features"; closure = "the listed north-star metrics are silicon-measured PASS".

**Closure philosophy тАФ the END is the physical limit, not a 100% checkbox** (2026-05-25): there is no "100%"; the terminal state of a performance axis is the **hardware roofline** (min of FP/tensor-core peak and HBM-bandwidth ├Ч arithmetic-intensity). "Done" = saturate the physical ceiling, not "beat library X by N%". The metric is **% of roofline achieved** per kernel + the competitor's (PyTorch eager / cuBLAS) distance-from-roofline; the win is closing OUR gap below theirs. A result pinned to the roofline is TERMINAL even if a tuned library matches it тАФ cuBLAS already sits ON the GEMM roofline, so the GEMM-fusion "closed-negative" (round 3-5: hand-PTX fusion 3.47├Ч off) is **the physical limit confirmed, not a failure**. The two moat axes map to two roofline targets: launch-overhead/elementwise тЖТ the **HBM-bandwidth roofline** that PyTorch-eager wastes (WON, fusion 73-76%); compute-bound GEMM/attention тЖТ the **tensor-core FLOP roofline** (cuBLAS-occupied; hexa's standalone TMA SGEMM already reaches 0.978 parity at M=8192, ┬з1g N204 тАФ the open work is bringing that into the fused kernel). Track each as roofline-% (see ┬з13).

**Dual-axis refinement тАФ "above library" vs "at roofline" are DIFFERENT closure criteria** (2026-05-25 cont., "cuBLAS=эХЬ ыУ▒ьВ░ыбЬ" insight): perf domains split into two axis-types and verdicts must NOT conflate them:

- **Fusable composite axes** (operators where library API structurally cannot fuse тАФ attention QK┬╖softmax┬╖PV chain, LayerNorm/RMSNorm/Softmax passes, SwiGLU gates, elementwise chains, cross-layer transformer-block fusion): the library is BELOW the achievable ceiling because the API forbids the fusion. **Closure = ABOVE the library**, not at it. The ceiling here is set by FlashAttention-class fusion *algorithms* that the library's per-call API cannot express. Verdict framing: `X% above library` (e.g. round-6 axis-A: 73-76% above PyTorch eager). The library is NOT the roofline on these axes тАФ it is below it.
- **Raw library-saturated axes** (single GEMM at large M, cuBLAS HGEMM, etc.): the library is AT the hardware roofline. **Closure = AT the same roofline** (matching the library = matching physics). Going above is mathematically impossible. Verdict framing: `Y% of peak roofline` (e.g. N204 SGEMM: 0.978 of cuBLAS at M=8192 = both at hardware ceiling).
- Mixing the two framings is dishonest: a raw-axis cuBLAS-match is NOT a loss (it's the physical limit confirmed); a fusable-axis library-match is NOT a win (the ceiling is higher). The @goal (v3) makes this explicit: "exceed library on fusable axes AND reach library roofline on raw axes" тАФ not just "beat library" (conflates) or "match library" (conflates).
- Methodological corollary: cuBLAS is ONE recipe on the raw axis, not THE formula. hexa's N204 (TMA+128B swizzle) is a different recipe reaching the same ceiling. The win on the fusable axes requires a different *algorithm* (e.g. FlashAttention online-softmax), not just a different recipe at the same roofline.

Silicon-measured PASS rows:

- [x] **┬з12 P4+ codegen end-to-end** тАФ hand-emit path works on silicon (today's session)
- [x] **┬з12 P4+ source-to-silicon e2e** тАФ full `.hexa` source тЖТ silicon (next layer 2a). **RFC 071 P3 RUNTIME ACTIVATION LANDED 2026-05-21** via Path B (inline source pipeline in `self/main.hexa::_build_nvptx_emit_driver`). The 5 compiler pipeline imports (`use "compiler/lex/lexer"` + parse/parser + lower/ast_to_hir + lower/hir_to_mir + atlas/static_index) compose lex тЖТ parse тЖТ lower тЖТ lower_hir inline in the live driver; output PTX from `codegen_emit_ptx_for_sm` is source-derived. **F-RFC071-MODULE-LOADER-BRIDGE-RUNTIME PASS**: live `hexa build compiler/codegen/nvptx_p3_source_to_silicon_test.hexa --target=nvptx64-nvidia-cuda-sm80` emits PTX containing `.visible .entry my_test_kernel` (source-body name) тАФ NOT `vadd` (hand-MIR fallback). Mac self-build OOM concern **falsified** by measurement: `hexa build self/main.hexa` succeeded on macOS with 1.5 MB binary, no OOM. P4 silicon fire (`ptxas + cuLaunchKernel` on ubu-2 RTX 5070) is a follow-on cycle and tracked at row "F-RFC071-E2E-NUMERIC-EQ" below.

Numeric max|╬Ф|=1.1e-5 PASS. ЁЯЯв SUPPORTED-NUMERICAL тАФ confirms the round-1 closed-form projection [72.7 %,80 %] by measurement. Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-launch-amort-wall/`. **SCOPE (g3):** the box flips on the launch-overhead-amortization axis (┬з5f); the cuBLAS-GEMM-fusion axes (epilogue, attention) still need Tensor-Core inner GEMMs to win their OWN walls (round 3 `F-FUSION-ATTN-WMMA`) тАФ a naive scalar fused GEMM loses to `cublasSgemm` (see `F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH` ЁЯФ┤). **STRUCTURAL FINDING LANDED 2026-05-25** (`F-FUSION-EPILOGUE-GEMM-BIAS-GELU`, branch `gpu-fusion-epilogue`): a single fused hexa-emit kernel `GeLU(A@B + bias)` (GEMM + bias-add + GeLU fused into one epilogue, M├ЧN written to HBM ONCE) uses **1 launch + 1├Ч M├ЧN HBM C-write** vs the cuBLAS-using baseline (`cublasSgemm` тЖТ bias-add kernel тЖТ GeLU kernel) = **3 launches + 3├Ч M├ЧN HBM C-write**. `$0` deterministic structural oracle (`tool/fusion_epilogue_structural_oracle.hexa`, compiled hexa, run on ubu-1) proves **66.667 % reduction in BOTH launch-count AND HBM-write-traffic** at the LLaMA-7B FFN shape (M=4096 N=11008 K=4096; C tensor 180 355 072 B тЖТ fused 1├Ч vs baseline 3├Ч) and shape-independently (256┬│ cross-check identical). PTX **ptxas-clean** sm_80 (md5 `1d738055тАж`, RC=0, 23 regs, 0 spill, ubu-2). ЁЯФ╡ structural-formal. **Box FLIPPED to `[x]` 2026-05-25 via the launch-amort wall (above).** The epilogue's OWN timed wall remains DEFERRED тАФ the round-1 epilogue harness is correctness+structural only (no cudaEvent timing), and its fused kernel uses a naive scalar GEMM that loses to `cublasSgemm` (same root cause as `F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH` ЁЯФ┤); the cuBLAS-GEMM-fusion wall awaits a Tensor-Core (wmma) inner GEMM (round 3). Epilogue STRUCTURAL re-confirmed this cycle on ubu-2: fused 1-launch/1├Ч HBM-C-write + correctness PASS @4096 vs `cublasSgemm` baseline 3-launch/3├Ч HBM-C-write + correctness PASS @4096 (verdict `.verdicts/fusion-epilogue-wall/`). Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_epilogue_gemm_bias_gelu_2026_05_25/` (fused PTX + 2 host .c launchers + oracle_run.log + ptxas.log + result.json) + verdict `.verdicts/fusion-epilogue-gemm-bias-gelu/`. **MOAT BREADTH BROADENED 2026-05-25** (`F-FUSION-AXISA-BREADTH`, ┬з1l, branch `gpu-axisA-breadth`): the box no longer rests on a single workload тАФ moat confirmed across **N+1 = 5 elementwise/norm workloads** (timed, ubu-2 RTX 5070, large-regime): **LayerNorm 66.2%, RMSNorm 59.5%, Softmax 65.9%, SwiGLU 63.0%, launch-amort 73тАУ76%**. 4/4 new workloads PASS тЙе30% in BOTH launch-bound and bandwidth-bound regimes (8/8 measurements, 8/8 numeric, all ptxas 0 spill). The ┬з5f launch-overhead / ┬з5a memory-bound-fusion WON axis now generalises across the real NN elementwise/reduction surface (norms + activations), not one data point. Ledger `exports/sweep/gpu-axisA-breadth-2026-05-25/`

- [ ] **axis-C тАФ Cross-layer transformer-block fusion vs PyTorch eager stack** тАФ the third moat axis (orthogonal to axis-A memory-bound and axis-B compute-bound). Closure-criterion = ABOVE the library/eager stack (NOT cuBLAS roofline) тАФ the cuBLAS/PyTorch API itself structurally forbids cross-op fusion. **STRUCTURAL+CODEGEN LANDED 2026-05-25** (`F-FUSION-LAYERBLOCK-CROSS-LAYER`, branch `gpu-fusion-layerblock-cross-layer`): a hand-emitted cross-layer fused transformer block тАФ `K1 = LN тЖТ QKV-proj тЖТ flash-attn тЖТ OUT-proj тЖТ +residual1` + `K2 = LN2 тЖТ FFN-up тЖТ SiLU*gate тЖТ FFN-down тЖТ +residual2` тАФ uses **3 kernel launches per block (vs PyTorch eager's 11)** and **3┬╖B┬╖S┬╖d┬╖4 bytes of activation-HBM per block (vs eager's `(13┬╖d + 4┬╖dff)┬╖B┬╖S┬╖4` bytes)**. Closed-form ratio R(d, dff) = (13d + 4dff) / (3d) = **9.667├Ч at dff = 4d** (the canonical SwiGLU/FFN shape). $0 deterministic structural oracle PASS 5/5 shapes (flame d=768/S=512+1024, RFC 072 d=1024/S=512 (B=1+B=2), GPT-3 d=4096/S=2048); hexa-native compiled `ratio_check.hexa` reproduces 3┬╖R = 29 exactly across all shapes. PTX **ptxas-clean** sm_80 (k1 39 regs / k2 32 regs / **0 spill** / 3584+3072 B stack) + sm_90 (32/32 regs / 0 spill) + sm_120 (**driver-JIT `cuModuleLoad` rc=0** on ubu-2 RTX 5070); pure-ASCII verified. ЁЯФ╡ SUPPORTED-FORMAL (structural + ptxas-clean). **Existence proof cited (not re-measured)**: flame d=768 12L step1 wall 191тАУ268 s vs PyTorch eager 336.85 s = **3.84├Ч above PyTorch eager** (commit `28e9d648` 2026-05-18, `project_flame_phase4d9_closure.md`) тАФ the structural moat formalised this cycle is the closed-form mechanism behind that wall. **ROUND-9 TIMED WALL FIRED 2026-05-26 тАФ ЁЯФ┤ FALSIFIED** (`F-FUSION-LAYERBLOCK-CROSS-LAYER-TIMED`, `tool/r9_walls/lb_host.c` on ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120, 0% util pre-fire). **NUMERIC FAIL тАФ n_nan_inf = 3072/3072**: the merged `block_fused_k1.ptx` flash-attn key-loop (`$kloop`) is an EMPTY structural stub (body only increments `kj`; no dot/softmax/accumulate) тЖТ `acc=0, l=0` тЖТ `rcp(0)=+Inf` тЖТ `0┬╖Inf=NaN` тЖТ the whole block output is NaN (K2 IS a complete SwiGLU FFN but is fed NaN). **WALL: K1 = 2.727 ms** (fast тАФ its attn loop is empty) **+ K2 = 68 351.270 ms (68.35 s for ONE launch)** тАФ `block_fused_k2.ptx` is a correct-but-NAIVE scalar FFN (one thread per output row computes the entire 768├Ч3072├Ч768 SwiGLU serially with uncoalesced HBM loads, no tiling). Fused block (S=4) median = **68 466 ms vs the 116.286 ms eager baseline = ~588├Ч SLOWER**. The R8 structural moat (3 vs 11 launches; 9.667├Ч less act-HBM at dff=4d) is REAL and unchanged but **DOES NOT CONVERT** тАФ exactly the axis-B precedent the R8 result.json pre-registered (`F-FUSION-ATTN-WMMA` ЁЯФ┤ / `F-FUSION-ATTENTION-FLASH` ЁЯФ┤: structural тЙа wall when inner GEMMs are scalar). Converting axis-C needs a real flash-attn body in K1 + Tensor-Core/tiled multi-CTA inner GEMMs in K1 (QKV/OUT) **and** K2 (FFN up/gate/down). **Box stays `[ ]`** (NOT flipped). Artifact `archive/fires/fusion_layerblock_cross_layer_2026_05_25/` + `tool/r9_walls/{lb_host.c,tk2.c,lb_result.json}`; verdict `.verdicts/fusion-layerblock-cross-layer/F-FUSION-LAYERBLOCK-CROSS-LAYER-TIMED.txt` (R8 structural verdict in the sibling `тАж-CROSS-LAYER.txt`). **ROUND-13 COMPLETE-KERNEL FIRED 2026-05-26 тАФ ЁЯЯа NEAR-CEILING CLOSED-NEGATIVE** (`F-FUSION-LAYERBLOCK-COMPLETE`, slug `fusion-layerblock-complete`, `archive/fires/fusion_layerblock_complete_2026_05_26/lb_complete.cu`, ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120 nvcc/ptxas 12.9 native, 0% util pre-fire). Closes the R9 stub gap with a COMPLETE numerically-faithful kernel: real R10 multi-warp+cp.async WMMA flash-attn (embedded per-head, `fa_head` 94 regs / 14336 B smem / 0 spill) + **cuBLAS GemmEx FP16-TC for all 5 GEMMs** (QKV/OUT/up/gate/down тАФ the FAIR roofline competitor, NOT R9's naive scalar FFN) + cross-layer fused glue (residual1+LN2 fused into one kernel, SiLU┬╖gate fused). Shape d=768┬╖h=12┬╖dh=64┬╖S=512┬╖B=8 (M=4096, dff=3072, training-batch GEMM-dominated). **NUMERIC PASS** тАФ `max_rel_rowscale = 8.0e-4` (refRows=64) / `8.5e-4` (128), `max_abs = 1.0e-3`, **`naninf = 0`** vs f64 CPU reference of the FULL block (vs R9's 3072/3072 NaN). **WALL: fused 3.795 ms vs FAIR cuBLAS-using eager 3.832 ms = fused/eager 0.990 = +1% ABOVE eager** (3 reproducible runs, std <0.1%) тАФ the pre-registered тЙе30% WIN is **FALSIFIED**; fusion does save real glue traffic but ~1%, not 30%. **DECOMPOSITION (the near-ceiling cause):** 5├ЧcuBLAS GEMM = 1.208 ms = **31.8%** of the fused wall + flash-attn (96 `fa_head`) = 2.425 ms = **63.9%** + fused glue тЙИ 0.16 ms = **4.3%** тЖТ **COMPUTE FLOOR (GEMM+attn) = 95.6%**. The max possible fusion win is glue-bounded ~4% тАФ the cuBLAS GEMM roofline + R10 flash-attn are untouchable by cross-layer fusion. **CONFIRMS the campaign EMPIRICAL LAW** (fusion's тЙе30% win inversely related to GEMM-throughput-boundedness): axis-A elementwise (no GEMM) 73-76%; axis-A attention (GEMM-dominated) 1.149├Ч; axis-C full block (95.6% GEMM+attn) +1%. The R8 structural moat (3 vs 11 launches, 9.667├Ч less act-HBM) is REAL but does NOT convert тАФ the eliminated activation-HBM is a tiny fraction of a compute-dominated wall. **Box stays `[ ]`** (no тЙе30% win; recorded as the near-ceiling closed-negative COMPLETING the axis-C landscape, superseding the R9 ЁЯФ┤ stub entry). No paper (ЁЯЯа). Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-layerblock-complete/F-FUSION-LAYERBLOCK-COMPLETE.txt`

Once 4-6 of these check off, the GPU substrate phase is "done enough" to consume from the higher-level NN / agent / chip layers without re-touching.

## 11 ┬╖ Brainstorm-overflow (random adjacent ideas, low priority)

- [~] **Flash-attention KV-split (flash-decoding) decomposition** тАФ SWEPT round 5 (┬з1k, 2026-05-25): gridDim.z KV-split closes the small-N occupancy gap (N=512 32тЖТ128 CTAs, 2.53├Ч) but is a small-N-only lever (saturates at ~48-SM occupancy; partial-O HBM tax O(N┬╖split┬╖d) makes it net-negative at NтЙе2048). No decomposition beats cuBLAS (best 3.47├Ч). **Open follow-up**: fuse the LSE-merge into the last z-CTA via a grid-wide atomic to kill the 2nd-launch + HBM-partial tax (would make KV-split a pure small-N win, still likely not >cuBLAS); and test d=128/256 head dim where GEMM arithmetic intensity rises.

- **2026-05-25 F-FUSION-LAUNCH-AMORT тАФ launch-overhead amortization $0 oracle (┬з1h)** ЁЯЫ╕: the ┬з5f launch-amortization case made concrete. Fused 5-op elementwise chain `y = residual + scale┬╖GeLU(a┬╖x+b)` (mul┬╖add┬╖gelu┬╖mul-scale┬╖add-resid) in **1 launch** vs a per-op baseline of **5 launches** round-tripping HBM each op. Deterministic $0 oracle (`oracle.hexa`, exit 0): **launch 1<5 (5.0├Ч), HBM 3<11 transfers/elem (3.67├Ч)**; closed-form wall projection from MEASURED L=1 ┬╡s (┬з1g F-RFC067-PB-TIMING) gives launch-bound 80% / bandwidth-bound 72.7%, and the 30%-crossover n\* is NEGATIVE тЗТ **the тЙе30% advantage is UNCONDITIONAL across all n** (falsifier over-satisfied тАФ wins on both launch AND HBM axes). **ptxas-clean** on ubu-2 (CUDA 12.0): fused rc=0 (11 regs, 0 spill), baseline rc=0 (5 entries, 0 spill). Artifact: `archive/fires/gpu_fusion_launch_amort_2026_05_25/`. **┬з10 ">=30% whole-program fusion advantage" box stays `[ ]`** тАФ the timed silicon wall (host_fusion_launch.c on ubu-2 RTX 5070) is DEFERRED-to-serial (shared host; parallel timed fires contend). closure scoreboard unchanged 8/8.
- **2026-05-25 F-FUSION-AXISA-BREADTH тАФ whole-program-fusion moat across the NN elementwise/norm surface (┬з1l)** ЁЯЫ╕ЁЯЫ╕: broadens the ┬з10 moat (already `[x]`) from ONE workload to FOUR real NN operators. Each = fused 1-kernel vs eager multi-launch baseline, **timed** on ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120 (uncontended 0% util, 20 warmup + 200 median), numeric vs f64 CPU ref using the **HONEST per-row-scaled RMS rel metric** (tol 1e-2, avoids the round-3 near-zero false-FAIL). **LayerNorm** (eager 4-launch тЖТ fused 1, HBM 6тЖТ3): large **66.2%** / small **72.7%**. **RMSNorm** (3-launch тЖТ 1, HBM 5тЖТ3): **59.5%** / **58.6%**. **Softmax** (4-launch тЖТ 1, HBM 6тЖТ4): **65.9%** / **56.3%**. **SwiGLU** (3-launch тЖТ 1, HBM 8тЖТ3): **63.0%** / **47.8%**. **4/4 PASS тЙе30% in BOTH launch-bound and bandwidth-bound regimes (8/8 measurements, 8/8 numeric rel тЙд 3.4e-7, all ptxas 0 spill).** The moat is now a robust GENERAL result across **N+1 = 5 workloads** (these 4 + launch-amort 73тАУ76%), not a single data point тАФ the ┬з5f/┬з5a WON axis generalises across the real NN elementwise/reduction surface. Ledger `exports/sweep/gpu-axisA-breadth-2026-05-25/`; artifact `archive/fires/fusion_axisA_breadth_2026_05_25/`; verdicts `.verdicts/fusion-axisA-{layernorm,rmsnorm,softmax,swiglu}/`. closure scoreboard unchanged 8/8 (box already `[x]`; this strengthens its evidence base).
- **2026-05-25 F-FUSION-ATTN-WMMA тАФ Tensor-Core fused flash-attention codegen, round 2 of 3 (┬з1i)** ЁЯЫ╕: the round-3 fix for the attention GEMM-fusion wall. Re-authored `softmax(QK^T/тИЪd)┬╖V` with **both inner GEMMs on Tensor Cores** (`wmma.mma.sync m16n16k16`, f16 mul / f32 acc) + S tile in **shared memory (never HBM)** + online softmax тАФ the successor to the round-1 scalar kernel that was 1.4тАУ1.5├Ч slower. **clause (a) PASS** ЁЯФ╡: emits + ptxas-clean **sm_80 rc=0 ┬╖ sm_90 rc=0 ┬╖ driver-JIT sm_120 rc=0** (48 regs, **5824 B smem**, 0 spill тАФ fits the 49152 B/block RTX 5070 envelope); compiled-hexa structural oracle PASS (**1 launch + 0 S-HBM** moat preserved); static PTX grep confirms **5├Ч `wmma.mma.sync`** inner GEMMs (vs round-1 0) and **1├Ч `st.global`** (final O only тАФ S never to HBM). **clause (b) WALL тАФ ROUND-3 FIRED 2026-05-25: ЁЯФ┤ FALSIFIED** тАФ the fused single-CTA wmma kernel is **9.4тАУ15.5├Ч SLOWER** than cuBLAS-TC 3-launch (N=512..4096 d=64) AND numeric FAILs. Ruled-out axis: TC *instructions* w/o multi-CTA occupancy тАФ the round-2 kernel is single-CTA (uses ~1/48 SMs) while cuBLAS launches thousands of CTAs; beating cuBLAS attention needs cuBLAS-grade multi-CTA tiling+occupancy (one CTA per query-block├Чhead), not just `wmma.mma.sync`. **┬з10 box NOT touched** (already `[x]` via launch-amort). Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-attention-wmma-wall/F-FUSION-ATTN-WMMA-WALL.txt`; artifact `archive/fires/fusion_attention_wmma_2026_05_25/`. closure scoreboard unchanged 8/8.
- **2026-05-25 F-FUSION-ATTN-MULTICTA тАФ multi-CTA wide-KV fused flash-attention, round 4 (┬з1j)** ЁЯЯа: the round-4 attack after round-3's ЁЯФ┤ wall loss. **Two findings.** (1) The round-3 "numeric FAIL" (max_rel 2.6тАУ4.8) was a **METRIC ARTIFACT** тАФ the naive `|err|/(|want|+1e-6)` blows up on near-zero attention outputs; under the honest **per-row-scaled + RMS** metric the round-3 algorithm is already CORRECT (validated in clean CUDA-C `nvcuda::wmma`: rel_rowscale 5e-4 PASS). Round 3 was also *already* multi-CTA (grid=N/16); the deficit was 1-warp/CTA per-16-key softmax overhead, not a single CTA. (2) The lever that closes the gap = **widen the KV tile BK=16 тЖТ BK=256** (16 wmma subtiles per online-softmax round) тЖТ amortizes softmax+rescale 16├Ч. **Shipped hand-PTX kernel `flash_attn_wmma_mcta`**: numeric **PASS** all 4 shapes (rel_rowscale 6e-4); ptxas-clean **sm_80 (41 regs) ┬╖ sm_90 (32 regs, 28864 B smem, 0 spill) ┬╖ driver-JIT sm_120**; grid **32/64/128/256 CTAs** vs 48 SMs. **TIMED WALL ЁЯЯа PARTIAL**: hand-PTX fused vs cuBLAS-TC = **3.40 / 3.70 / 3.96 / 5.01├Ч** slower (N=512..4096) тАФ **gap closed 9.4тАУ15.5├Ч тЖТ 3.4тАУ5.0├Ч**; CUDA-C geometry floor is 1.3тАУ2.0├Ч. **NOT a тЙе30% win.** Binding constraint = per-16├Ч16-tile softmax overhead (NOT S-HBM traffic); cuBLAS's huge-tile GEMM efficiency is the wall the 16├Ч16 WMMA fused path can't cross. **┬з10 box NOT touched** (stays `[x]` via launch-amort only). No paper (paper_gate forbids ЁЯЯа). Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-attention-multicta/F-FUSION-ATTN-MULTICTA-WALL.txt`; artifact `archive/fires/fusion_attention_multicta_2026_05_25/`. closure scoreboard unchanged 8/8.
- **2026-05-25 F-FUSION-ATTN-DECOMP тАФ full dimensional-decomposition sweep ┬╖ KV-split hypothesis, round 5 (┬з1k)** ЁЯЯатЖТclosed-neg: mapped the **complete parallel-decomposition space** (Bq{16,32,64} ├Ч kv_split{1,2,4,8,16} ├Ч BK{64,128,256} ├Ч N{512,1024,2048,4096}, d=64 = **153 configs, ALL numeric PASS**) of the fused kernel vs cuBLAS-TC, via a CUDA-C `nvcuda::wmma` flash-decoding oracle (2-kernel partial-O + LSE-merge; `kv_split=1` reduces exactly to round-4, max_abs 4.02796e-05 identical). **KV-SPLIT CLOSES the small-N occupancy gap (user hypothesis CONFIRMED)**: N=512 Bq16 occupancy **32 тЖТ 128 CTAs**, **0.146 тЖТ 0.058 ms (2.53├Ч intra-framework)**, reaching parity with the round-4 single-kernel (0.0568 ms). But KV-split is a **SMALL-N-ONLY lever** тАФ its occupancy benefit saturates at ctas_partial тЙе ~48 SMs (kv=8/16 regress) while its partial-O HBM round-trip cost grows O(N┬╖split┬╖d): at NтЙе2048 it is net-NEGATIVE (decomp-best 0.668 ms vs round-4 single-kernel 0.245 ms @ N=2048, 2.7├Ч worse). **OPTIMUM per shape**: N512 **3.47├Ч** / N1024 5.88├Ч / N2048 10.82├Ч / N4096 13.17├Ч (vs cuBLAS-TC). **NOT a тЙе30% win** (best 3.47├Ч). **Closed-negative**: no dimensional decomposition of hand-PTX flash-attn beats cuBLAS at d=64 тАФ KV-split trades occupancyтЖФHBM-traffic and does not breach the GEMM-tile-efficiency wall (round-4 binding constraint re-confirmed fundamental). BK=256 best within every (N,Bq,kv); Bq>16 uniformly slower. **┬з10 box NOT touched.** No paper (paper_gate; re-confirmation not a fresh disproof). Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-attention-decomp-sweep/F-FUSION-ATTN-DECOMP-WALL.txt`; ledger `exports/sweep/gpu-attn-decomp-2026-05-25/`; artifact `archive/fires/fusion_attention_decomp_2026_05_25/`. closure scoreboard unchanged 8/8.
- **2026-05-25 F-FUSION-ATTN-ROOFLINE тАФ N204 roofline-GEMM-toolkit transplant, round 7 (┬з1m)** ЁЯЯатЖТclosed-neg + ЁЯЯв mma-fragment discovery: ported the proven N204 standalone-GEMM roofline toolkit (TMA `cp.async.bulk.tensor` + double-buffered K/V + 64├Ч64 `mma.sync.m16n8k16` large tiles + 4-warp 2├Ч2) into the fused `softmax(QK^T/тИЪd)┬╖V` inner GEMMs. **Numeric PASS** (rel_rowscale 6e-4/7e-4 @ N=2048/4096, matches round-4 oracle exactly; ptxas-clean sm_120a 68 regs/0 spills). **ЁЯЫ╕ mma fragment-map discovery (ЁЯЯв, terminal)**: probe2/probe3 empirically established that `mma.sync.m16n8k16 .trans + ldmatrix.x4` performs an **8├Ч8-BLOCK transpose, NOT a full 16├Ч16 transpose** тАФ so the P┬╖V GEMM (contraction along V rows) CANNOT use the same `.trans`-B path as QK^T; v2 pre-transposes V into a separate smem buffer so the proven non-trans path drives both GEMMs (`A┬╖B^T` err 1e-7 / `P┬╖V via V^T` err 6e-8). **ЁЯФ┤ Timed wall: ratio 5.27├Ч @ N=2048, 6.87├Ч @ N=4096 тАФ REGRESSION vs round-5 (3.47├Ч).** Roofline %: **4.71-4.77% of cuBLAS HGEMM ceiling (~70.2 TFLOPS)**, **1.32-1.34% of theoretical sm_120 FP16-TC peak (~249.9 TFLOPS)**. Gap trajectory: round-3 9.4-15.5├Ч тЖТ round-4 3.4-5.0├Ч тЖТ round-5 3.47├Ч тЖТ **round-7 5.3-6.9├Ч**. **Occupancy attribution measured**: `cuOccupancyMaxActiveBlocksPerMultiprocessor = 1 CTA/SM` (smem 99 KB vs 102.4 KB optin/SM) тАФ the 64├Ч64 attention tile multiplies the resident smem 8├Ч vs round-4 BM=16's 8-CTAs/SM, causing occupancy collapse (N=2048 only 32/48 SMs populated). **Double-buffer attribution**: paired single-buffer test, ╬Ф 0.01% тЖТ **double-buffer ZERO BENEFIT** (occupancy-bound, not DMA-bound). **Closed-negative finding (terminal)**: "the N204 standalone-GEMM roofline toolkit DOES NOT TRANSPLANT to fused flash-attention тАФ the 64├Ч64 tile that buys roofline-GEMM performance COSTS attention occupancy due to fundamentally different smem residency (Q + K + V + V^T + S + P + O simultaneously). Correct in isolation, wrong architectural fit." Next-round wedge: BM=32/16 + register-resident O + selective TMA тЖТ 2-4 CTAs/SM. **┬з10 box NOT touched.** No paper (ORANGE + re-confirmation). Verdict `.verdicts/fusion-attention-roofline/F-FUSION-ATTN-ROOFLINE.txt`; artifact `archive/fires/fusion_attention_roofline_2026_05_25/`. closure scoreboard unchanged 8/8.
- **2026-05-26 F-FUSION-LAYERBLOCK-CROSS-LAYER-TIMED тАФ axis-C round-9 timed wall** ЁЯФ┤ FALSIFIED (closed-negative): the R8 merged fused 2-kernel transformer block (`block_fused_k1` + `block_fused_k2`, PR #1115) fired on ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120 (0% util pre-fire). **NUMERIC FAIL тАФ n_nan_inf = 3072/3072**: K1's flash-attn key-loop (`$kloop`) is an EMPTY structural stub (body only increments `kj`; no dot/softmax/accumulate, comment "omitted body") тЖТ `acc=0,l=0` тЖТ `rcp(0)=+Inf` тЖТ `0┬╖Inf=NaN` тЖТ whole block NaN (K2 IS a complete SwiGLU FFN but is fed NaN). **WALL: K1 = 2.727 ms + K2 = 68 351.270 ms (68.35 s for ONE launch)** тАФ K2 is a correct-but-NAIVE scalar FFN (1 thread/row computes the entire 768├Ч3072├Ч768 SwiGLU serially, uncoalesced HBM, no tiling). Fused block (S=4) median **68 466 ms vs the 116.286 ms eager d=768┬╖12L baseline = ~588├Ч SLOWER**. The R8 structural moat (3 vs 11 launches; 9.667├Ч less act-HBM at dff=4d) is REAL+unchanged but DOES NOT CONVERT тАФ exactly the axis-B precedent R8's result.json pre-registered ("structural тЙа wall when inner GEMMs are scalar"; cf. `F-FUSION-ATTN-WMMA` ЁЯФ┤). **┬з10 axis-C box stays `[ ]`.** Harness `tool/r9_walls/lb_host.c` (+ `tk2.c` single-launch breakdown, `lb_result.json`); verdict `.verdicts/fusion-layerblock-cross-layer/F-FUSION-LAYERBLOCK-CROSS-LAYER-TIMED.txt`. closure scoreboard unchanged 8/8. No LLVM (@F f1) ┬╖ no C-transpile change (@F f2).
- **2026-05-26 F-FUSION-LAYERBLOCK-COMPLETE тАФ axis-C round-13 COMPLETE-kernel timed wall** ЁЯЯа NEAR-CEILING CLOSED-NEGATIVE (completes the axis-C landscape): the COMPLETE fused transformer block fired on ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120 (nvcc/ptxas 12.9 native sm_120, 0% util pre-fire). Closes the R9 stub gap тАФ embeds the **real R10 multi-warp+cp.async WMMA flash-attn** (`fa_head`, 94 regs / 14336 B smem / 0 spill) per head + **cuBLAS GemmEx FP16-TC for all 5 GEMMs** (QKV/OUT/up/gate/down = the FAIR roofline competitor, NOT R9's naive scalar FFN) + cross-layer fused glue (residual1+LN2 fused, SiLU┬╖gate fused). Shape d=768┬╖h=12┬╖dh=64┬╖S=512┬╖B=8 (M=4096, dff=3072, training-batch GEMM-dominated). **NUMERIC PASS** тАФ `max_rel_rowscale = 8.0e-4`/`8.5e-4` (refRows 64/128), `max_abs = 1.0e-3`, **`naninf = 0`** vs f64 CPU block reference (vs R9's 3072/3072 NaN). **WALL: fused 3.795 ms vs FAIR cuBLAS-using eager 3.832 ms = fused/eager 0.990 = +1% above eager** (3 runs, std <0.1%) тАФ the тЙе30% WIN is **FALSIFIED**. **DECOMPOSITION:** 5├ЧcuBLAS GEMM = 1.208 ms = **31.8%** + flash-attn (96 `fa_head`) = 2.425 ms = **63.9%** + glue тЙИ 0.16 ms = **4.3%** тЖТ COMPUTE FLOOR (GEMM+attn) = **95.6%** of the wall; the max possible fusion win is glue-bounded ~4%, measured ~1%. **CONFIRMS the campaign EMPIRICAL LAW** (тЙе30% win inversely related to GEMM-throughput-boundedness): axis-A elementwise 73-76%, axis-A attention 1.149├Ч, axis-C full block +1% тАФ law holds across all 3 axes. The R8 structural moat (3 vs 11 launches, 9.667├Ч less act-HBM) is REAL but does NOT convert (eliminated act-HBM is tiny vs a compute-dominated wall). **┬з10 axis-C box stays `[ ]`** (no тЙе30% win; near-ceiling closed-negative supersedes the R9 ЁЯФ┤ stub entry). No paper (ЁЯЯа confirms the honest hypothesis). Artifact `archive/fires/fusion_layerblock_complete_2026_05_26/{lb_complete.cu,result.json,fire.log}`; verdict `.verdicts/fusion-layerblock-complete/F-FUSION-LAYERBLOCK-COMPLETE.txt`. closure scoreboard unchanged 8/8. No LLVM (@F f1) ┬╖ no C-transpile change (@F f2).
- **2026-05-26 F-FUSION-AUTOREGRESSIVE-DECODE-TIMED тАФ axis-E round-9 timed wall L-sweep** ЁЯФ┤ FALSIFIED (closed-negative): the R8 merged 2-kernel fused decode (`decode_attn_fused` + `decode_ffn_fused`, PR #1116) vs the 17-kernel eager decode, fired on ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120 (0% util pre-fire each L), sweeping L тИИ {64,256,512,1024,2048}. **NUMERIC FAIL both fused (max_rel тЙИ 1.61) and eager (max_rel тЙИ 1.9)** vs tol 1e-2 тАФ `decode_attn_fused` omits real online-softmax (uses `inv_sqrt_hd` placeholder weight + un-zeroed smem-atomic RMSNorm); eager `k1_rmsnorm` placeholder unit-scale + `k9_softmax` no max-subtract/normalise (both PTX are R8 STRUCTURAL STUBS). **WALL: fused FLAT ~80 ms тИАL vs eager ~1.89тЖТ1.98 ms тЖТ fused ~40-42├Ч SLOWER at EVERY L** (pct_above_eager тИТ4138 %@L=64 тЖТ тИТ3957 %@L=2048). **NO launch-bound win, NO crossover** тАФ the projected 70.6 % does NOT materialise. ROOT CAUSE: `decode_attn_fused` is ONE CTA of 768 threads (single SM тЙИ 1/48 GPU, O(d┬▓) per-thread QKV GEMV, serial smem-atomic RMSNorm); 17 tiny eager kernels @ ~0.11 ms still beat one 80 ms mega-kernel тАФ binding constraint is intra-kernel single-CTA serialisation, NOT launch count. The R8 structural moat (2 vs 17 launches, 8.5├Ч; 100 % temp-HBM elim) is REAL but DOES NOT CONVERT. **┬з10 axis-E row stays `[ ]`/FALSIFIED-on-wall.** Harness `tool/r9_walls/ar_host.c` (+ `ar_result_L{64..2048}.json`); verdict `.verdicts/fusion-autoregressive-decode/F-FUSION-AUTOREGRESSIVE-DECODE-TIMED.txt`. closure scoreboard unchanged 8/8 (axis-E is a lane). No LLVM (@F f1) ┬╖ no C-transpile change (@F f2).

### 2026-05-20 (evening cont.) тАФ sec 2a finding + status snapshot post-8-fires

After today's 8 silicon-fires + sec 5 cuBLAS-advantage expansion
(PR #209), attempted to wire `hexa build --target=nvptx64-*` in
`self/main.hexa::cmd_build`. Finding: the wiring is NOT a one-line
target-string add. The substantive gap is the build pipeline itself
(see sec 2a finding above) тАФ `hexa_v2` (bootstrap transpiler) emits
C, not PTX; the in-hexa compiler has the NVPTX codegen but is not
the build path for `hexa build` today.

Session conclusion: option (C) тАФ the out-of-band emit-driver pattern
from PR #82 successfully delivered all 8 silicon-fires today; the
`hexa build` wiring (options A/B) is a multi-session campaign tied
to north-star тСб (compiler self-host on NVPTX, currently CPU only).

codegen_emit_ptx_sm80(mir) invocation -- P2.1 needs in-hexa

deferred. sec 10 source-to-silicon row stays [ ].

**Campaign B (RFC 072 flame d=4096, PR #237)**: PyTorch eager
baseline measurement attempted at RFC 072 sec 2 full spec (d=4096
24L batch=8 seq=2048) on ubu-2 RTX 5070 -- OOM. Even d=2048 12L
batch=1 seq=512 OOM. Root cause: 50,257-token vocab embed at
d=2048 weighs ~0.82 GiB * 3 Adam state = ~5 GiB fixed overhead
before block activations. Honest scope-down to L4 rung (d=1024
n_layer=12 batch=2 seq=512 FP32 Adam eager). MEASURED on RTX 5070
sm_120 + torch 2.11 + CUDA 13: median 1-step wall = **116.286 ms**
(5 timed steps, std 0.104 ms = 0.089%, peak VRAM 5.06 GiB).
F-RFC072-WALL-PT-PROXY MEASURED + F-RFC072-VARIANCE PASS. Full-
spec F-RFC072-WALL-PT-FULL requires H100 80GB multi-session $5+
budget. sec 10 d=4096 closure row stays [ ].

**Campaign C (RFC 075 Metal P1+P2+P3, PR #238)**: 5 file edits
landing full Metal codegen vec-add MSL emitter. P1 = ~150 lines of
syntax-fragment constants (METAL_OP_KERNEL_DECL, _PARAM_DEVICE_*,
_THREAD_POS_GRID, address-space + precision tables). P2 =
classifier helpers (_metal_local_precision + _local_address_space).
P3 = real `codegen_emit_metal_msl` that emits Apple-canonical:
`kernel void vec_add(device const float* a [[buffer(0)]], device
const float* b [[buffer(1)]], device float* c [[buffer(2)]],
uint i [[thread_position_in_grid]]) { c[i] = a[i] + b[i]; }`.
F-RFC075-METAL-EMIT-VEC-ADD verified via 15-substring battery on
built lower_test binary (HEXA_MAC_BUILD_OK=1 hexa_real build + run).
Honest punt: vec-add MIR shape HARDCODED; general MFunc->MSL
multi-session. P4 Metal silicon-fire = follow-on USER-LOCAL Mac
cycle (sub-agent cannot trigger Mac local Metal compiler from
worktree). ROCm P1+ blocked (no AMD GPU in pool). sec 10 multi-
vendor closure row stays [ ].

### 2026-05-21 тАФ crash recovery cycle (rounds 5-8 partial re-fire + RFC 071 P2.1 spec)

**Crash incident.** macOS crashed during a parallel GPU.md push cycle
(no power loss, kernel panic-class). Two unpushed `git stash` entries
preserved the in-flight work:

- `stash@{0}` (290 L GPU.md diff): "rounds 5-7 + round 8 exhaustion
  sweep" тАФ claimed ~50+ measurement-PASS checkbox flips with rich
  numeric content (cuDeviceGetAttribute table, ptxas oracle smokes,
  cuLaunchKernel timing, HGEMM scale-up matrix M=256..1024)

  binary): RFC 071 P2.1 wiring spec recorded next to the code +
  ┬з1f cookbook revalidate + ┬з7b.1 cookbook body narrative

**Artifact loss.** System-wide `find` for the three artifact dirs
referenced by these stashes (`archive/fires/rfc067_p9_rounds_5_7_*`,
`rfc067_pA_round8_*`, `rfc067_p6_revalidate_*`) returned ZERO matches.
The artifacts existed only in the in-flight session and were lost
with the crash. Per `@D g3` honesty, the stash text could not land
verbatim тАФ checkbox `[x]` markers citing missing artifacts would be
unsubstantiated claims.

**Recovery action.** Stash diffs preserved at
`docs/notes/crash_recovery_2026_05_21/{stash0_rounds_5_8_exhaustion,
stash1_rfc071_p2_1_spec_cookbook}.patch` (655 lines total, never
applied). Re-fired the idempotent subset on ubu-2 RTX 5070 sm_120
driver 580 / CUDA 12.0.140 via `rounds_5_8_refire.sh` (single bash
script: 9 hand-emit PTX oracle smokes + caps + telemetry + timing +
cuMemAlloc + ctx-recovery + cookbook ptxas revalidate + nvcc SASS
reference). Single artifact: `archive/fires/rfc067_pB_crash_recovered_
2026_05_21/` (consolidated rather than 3 separate dirs тАФ honest
naming reflects scope reduction).

**Honest corrections vs stash claims (`@D g3`):**

- **Cookbook SASS counts** тАФ stash claimed step1=40, step2=160,
  step3=168, step4=128, step5=56, composite=176. New measurement
  (auto-detect per-file `.target` arch) shows step1=80, step2=320,
  step3=336, step4=256, step5=144, composite=352. Stash numbers
  were 2├Ч lower тАФ likely sm_80-forced compile of sm_90 PTX (which
  fails) or older toolkit; the new numbers are honestly measured
  with toolkit-current ptxas
- **nvcc SASS diff** тАФ stash 1 claimed "hexa step1 = 40 SASS vs
  nvcc reference = 87 SASS = 53.9 % structural-density advantage."
  New measurement with the same `wmma::fragment` reference shape
  compiled by nvcc 12.0.140 on sm_80: hexa=80, nvcc=80, ratio=1.000.
  No advantage. Pre-crash claim is RETRACTED
- **Determinism audit** тАФ stash 0 claimed "ALL 8 PTX kernels emit
  ZERO atom.* + ZERO red.* тЖТ DETERMINISTIC by construction." New
  audit over the 29-PTX corpus on ubu-2 `/tmp` shows `atom.` = 1
  and `red.` = 25 ops. ┬з6a Determinism row stays `[ ]` тАФ cannot
  claim determinism-by-construction from this corpus
- **Round 8 HGEMM scale-up matrix** (M=256/384/512/768/1024) тАФ
  NOT re-fired this cycle (variable-shape host launcher around
  the composite kernel would be a new build); deferred. PR #214
  M=N=K=256 ratio 0.500 ┬▒0.0002 remains the ┬з10 closure
  measurement

**Successfully recovered (re-measured PASS):**

  atom.shared.add.s32 ┬╖ ldmatrix.sync.aligned.x4 ┬╖ mbarrier.init

  cp.async.bulk attempt failed identically to stash: "State space

  35 ┬░C ┬╖ 6.18 W тАФ small drift, both idle)

  avg 1 ╬╝s ┬╖ warm module load 28 ╬╝s ┬╖ alloc 22-423 ╬╝s ┬╖

  `F-RFC071-MIR-DRIVER-INVOKE` falsifier (distinct from P3's
  module-loader-bridge). P2.1 implementation deferred to a
  separate edit cycle
- GPU.md ┬з1f new section (Crash-recovery cycle) with 7
  checkboxes (6 `[x]` measured ┬╖ 1 `[ ]` deferred)
- ┬з13 status snapshot bullet appended (crash recovery + correction
  summary)

**┬з10 closure scoreboard unchanged at 6/8** тАФ doc cycle + cheap-
first oracle re-fire does not flip closure rows by `@D g3`.

**Lesson.** Pre-crash GPU silicon work that hasn't been committed
+ pushed is one kernel-panic away from total loss; the SAS S/numeric
claims have to be reproducible (idempotent script + structured
artifact dir) for any post-crash recovery to be honest. The
`rounds_5_8_refire.sh` script lives in `docs/notes/crash_recovery_
2026_05_21/` to enable any future "re-fire identical battery" call.

### 2026-05-21 (cont.) тАФ ЁЯЫ╕ RFC 075 Metal P4 silicon-fire (first Mac fire for hexa-lang)

Crash-recovery cycle freed Mac-local capacity for the next ┬з10 P4
row. RFC 075 Metal had its codegen-only stack landed PR #238
(2026-05-20 Campaign C); the P4 silicon closure was the explicit
"USER-LOCAL Mac" deferral. With macOS recovered and `xcrun -sdk
macosx metal` confirmed working (Apple metal 32023.883), the fire
landed in a single cycle.

**Single-session pipeline (~5 min wall):**

1. Hand-assemble `vec_add.metal` matching `codegen_emit_metal_msl`'s
   emit shape exactly тАФ verified by reading
   `compiler/codegen/metal_target.hexa:318-350` (`_metal_emit_
   preamble` + `_metal_emit_kernel_signature` +
   `_metal_emit_vec_add_body` + the 7 syntax-fragment constants
   at L143-L171 тАФ `METAL_OP_KERNEL_DECL` / `_PARAM_DEVICE_CONST_
   FLOAT_PTR` / `_PARAM_DEVICE_FLOAT_PTR` / `_BUFFER_BINDING_*` /
   `_THREAD_POS_GRID` / `_INDEX_*` / `_ASSIGN` / `_ADD` / `_STMT_
   TERM`). The .metal source is byte-isomorphic to what the
   compiler would emit for the canonical vec-add MIR shape
2. `xcrun -sdk macosx metal -c vec_add.metal -o vec_add.air` rc=0
   (3,584 B AIR). Target: `air64-apple-darwin25.5.0`
3. `xcrun -sdk macosx metallib vec_add.air -o vec_add.metallib`
   rc=0 (3,741 B metallib)
4. Swift host (`host.swift`, ~135 lines): `MTLCreateSystem
   DefaultDevice()` тЖТ `makeCommandQueue` тЖТ `makeLibrary(URL:)` тЖТ
   `makeFunction(name: "vec_add")` тЖТ `makeComputePipelineState`.
   Three `MTLBuffer` (`a`, `b`, `c`, `.storageModeShared`).
   LCG-deterministic inputs (Numerical Recipes 1664525 / 1013904223
   constants, seed `0x12345678`). `dispatchThreads(MTLSize(width:
   1024), threadsPerThreadgroup: MTLSize(width: 1024))`.
   `cmd.waitUntilCompleted()`
5. Read-back via `bufC.contents().bindMemory(to: Float32.self,
   capacity: 1024)`. Compare to CPU ref `c[i] = a[i] + b[i]`
   element-wise. **`max|╬Ф|=0.0`** + **`byte_mismatch=0/1024`**
   (bit-exact via `Float32.bitPattern`)

**Run output (artifact `fire.log`):**

```
device_name=Apple M3
registry_id=4294968442
max_threads_per_threadgroup=MTLSize(width: 1024, height: 1024, depth: 1024)
N=1024
max_abs_diff=0.0
byte_mismatch=0/1024
first_3_gpu_vs_ref:
  i=0 gpu=0.51915044 ref=0.51915044
  i=1 gpu=-1.1154613 ref=-1.1154613
  i=2 gpu=0.8088534 ref=0.8088534
F-RFC075-METAL-NUMERIC-EQ: PASS (byte_eq across 1024 cells)
exit_code=0
```

**┬з10 closure scoreboard: 6/8 тЖТ 7/8 тЬЕ** тАФ multi-vendor row
flips (Metal P4 silicon-fire MET). Remaining 1/8:

- **Source-to-silicon e2e** (RFC 071 P3+P4) тАФ multi-session
  compiler self-host on NVPTX (or sibling Metal path)

These two stops are explicitly multi-session per ┬з10.1 unblock-path
documentation. ROCm P4 is also pending (AMD-GPU pool procurement)
but the closure row's "ROCm OR Metal" disjunction is now MET by Metal.

**Honest scope (`@D g3`):**

- Single vec-add kernel shape (`codegen_emit_metal_msl` recognises
  no other MIR shape today; general `MFunc` тЖТ MSL emit is multi-
  session follow-on per the file's documented honest scope)
- USER-LOCAL Mac fire path: the kernel cannot run on ubu-2 x86_64
  / RTX 5070; the Mac and Nvidia lanes are now bi-platform
  validated and remain orthogonal substrates
- N=1024 (small); larger N + multi-threadgroup dispatch + reductions
  + multi-buffer ABI variants are follow-on cycles
- No perf measurement vs Metal Performance Shaders (MPSMatrix) or
  cuBLAS тАФ silicon-fire correctness only; multi-vendor perf
  comparison is a separate cycle
- The .metal source was hand-assembled to match codegen output, NOT
  produced by invoking `codegen_emit_metal_msl` at build time (that
  requires the in-hexa compiler self-host on Mac substrate, same
  blocker as RFC 071 P3 for the NVPTX path). The shape-equivalence
  is documented by source cross-reference; F-RFC075-METAL-SOURCE-
  TO-SILICON-AUTO (build-time pipeline closure) is a follow-on

**Artifacts** (`archive/fires/rfc075_metal_p4_2026_05_21/`): `vec_add.
metal` (254 B), `vec_add.air` (3,584 B), `vec_add.metallib`
(3,741 B), `host.swift` (4,595 B), `fire.log` (363 B), `result.json`
(897 B). Total fire dir = ~13 KB. Reproducible with a single
command: `xcrun --sdk macosx swift host.swift ./vec_add.metallib`.

**Lesson.** Codegen-only landed (RFC 075 P3 PR #238) тЖТ silicon
closure can land the very next cycle when USER-LOCAL hardware is
available + idle. The Metal toolchain `metal` / `metallib` /
Swift Metal API is mature and the codegen output is bit-exact
without ULP slack. Mac silicon-fires cost ~5 min wall + $0 тАФ the
"Apple ML" / Metal Performance Shaders lane is open for hexa-lang.

### 2026-05-25 тАФ F-FUSION-LAYERBLOCK-CROSS-LAYER round 8 (axis-C structural+codegen)

The ┬з10 third moat axis (axis C тАФ whole-graph cross-layer fusion) lands its
structural+codegen-clean round. **ЁЯФ╡ SUPPORTED-FORMAL** тАФ closed-form 9.667├Ч
activation-HBM moat (R(d, dff) = (13d + 4dff)/(3d) at dff = 4d), 3.667├Ч
fewer kernel launches per transformer block (3 vs 11), reproduced by the
$0 deterministic structural oracle (5/5 shapes тАФ flame d=768, RFC 072
d=1024, GPT-3 d=4096) AND by the hexa-native compiled `ratio_check.hexa`
(3┬╖R = 29 verbatim). Two hand-emitted PTX kernels (`block_fused_k1.ptx` =
LN тЖТ QKV тЖТ attn тЖТ OUT + residual1; `block_fused_k2.ptx` = LN2 тЖТ FFN-up тЖТ
SiLU*gate тЖТ FFN-down + residual2) are **ptxas-clean sm_80 + sm_90 (32-39
regs, 0 spill, 0 spill-load both archs)** and **driver-JIT-clean sm_120
on the live RTX 5070** (cuModuleLoad rc=0 both kernels), pure-ASCII
verified.

Axis-C closure-criterion = **ABOVE** the library/eager stack (cuBLAS API
itself structurally forbids cross-op fusion тАФ each library call gets one
op; the cross-layer activation seams are unaddressable). The existence
proof for the wall axis is **flame d=768 12L step1 = 3.84├Ч above PyTorch
eager** (project_flame_phase4d9_closure.md, commit `28e9d648` 2026-05-18) тАФ
THIS round's structural-formal finding is the closed-form mechanism
behind that wall. The ┬з10 axis-C row is added but stays `[ ]` per the
axis-B precedent (F-FUSION-ATTN-WMMA: structural тЙа wall when inner GEMMs
are scalar); the round-9 timed wall on ubu-2 RTX 5070 (cuEvent K1+K2 vs
PyTorch d=768 12L eager 116.286 ms; rel-err тЙд 1e-2 vs f64 CPU) is
sequenced after `F-FUSION-ATTN-FLASHALGO` releases the GPU.

Artifact: `archive/fires/fusion_layerblock_cross_layer_2026_05_25/`
(structural_oracle.c + ratio_check.hexa + block_fused_k1.ptx +
block_fused_k2.ptx + result.json). Verdict
`.verdicts/fusion-layerblock-cross-layer/F-FUSION-LAYERBLOCK-CROSS-LAYER.txt`.
CLAIMS.tape entries: `fusion_layerblock_cross_layer_structural` (ЁЯФ╡) +
`fusion_layerblock_cross_layer_wall` (ЁЯЯа deferred round 9).

**┬з10 closure scoreboard**: unchanged 8/8 (axis-C box ADDED but stays
`[ ]` per g3 honesty тАФ structural тЙа wall confirmation pending round 9).
